
-----title
许昌 (出生地)

ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1044&endYear=1044')">1044年</a>　归许昌，丁父忧。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1045&endYear=1045')">1045年</a>　隐居许昌，丁父忧。作品：《感季夏南堂怀江十苏二》<div id='poem_244761' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_244761' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/244761?labeling=true' target='_blank'>感季夏南堂怀江十苏二</a><span class='authorDate'>（1045年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34428, "北宋", "韩维", "poem_title_244761")'>韩维</a></span><br id='poem_sentence_0_244761'>积雨漂暑馀，凉风作秋先。<div id='poem_sentence_0_244761_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_244761'>南堂草木深，蝉蜩嘒篱掾。<div id='poem_sentence_1_244761_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_244761'>感此时节流，坐伤人事变。<div id='poem_sentence_2_244761_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_244761'>去年居京华，晨昏侍亲燕。<div id='poem_sentence_3_244761_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_244761'>问谁过我频，江苏实邦彦。<div id='poem_sentence_4_244761_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_244761'>一朝艰祸缠，衔哀走穷县。<div id='poem_sentence_5_244761_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_244761'>形骸悲瘵中，气息仅如线。<div id='poem_sentence_6_244761_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_244761'>邻几谪官去，门征校亏羡。<div id='poem_sentence_7_244761_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_244761'>子美亦远游，江湖一蓬转。<div id='poem_sentence_8_244761_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_244761'>人生哀乐间，瞥若过目电。<div id='poem_sentence_9_244761_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_244761'>念此不敢已，淋漓泪垂面。<div id='poem_sentence_10_244761_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_244761'>二君希代宝，宁久世俗贱。<div id='poem_sentence_11_244761_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_244761'>天和酌无竭，玉德莫愈见。<div id='poem_sentence_12_244761_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_244761'>何以慰相思，酬篇伫来绚。<div id='poem_sentence_13_244761_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_244761'></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_244761_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1046&endYear=1046')">1046年</a>　隐居许昌，结识梅尧臣，唱和颇多。作品：《览梅圣俞诗编》《和圣俞饮会之作》《饮圣俞西轩》<div id='poem_244639' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_244639' class='poemTitle class='poemContent' id='poem_content_244639'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_244639'>夙昔诵佳句，跂予慕高风。<div id='poem_sentence_0_244639_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_244639'>何意忧艰馀，邂逅此相逢。<div id='poem_sentence_1_244639_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_244639'>君初应府辟，捧檄来自东。<div id='poem_sentence_2_244639_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_244639'>引车穷檐下，眷然顾微躬。<div id='poem_sentence_3_244639_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_244639'>姿表穆以秀，纯德信内充。<div id='poem_sentence_4_244639_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_244639'>乃知文章作，中与性情通。<div id='poem_sentence_5_244639_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_244639'>煌煌新诗章，垂光照昏蒙。<div id='poem_sentence_6_244639_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_244639'>启椟挹荆璞，引莛撞景钟。<div id='poem_sentence_7_244639_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_244639'><span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_8_244639", 244639, "Clauses/16/Comments/0")'>高篇</span>屡云阕，远思殊未终。<div id='poem_sentence_8_244639_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_244639'>譬如巧<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_9_244639", 244639, "Clauses/18/Comments/0")'>琴师</span>，哀弹发丝桐。<div id='poem_sentence_9_244639_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_244639'>中有冲淡意，要以心志穷。<div id='poem_sentence_10_244639_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_244639'>顾惟昧者听，莫辨徵与宫。<div id='poem_sentence_11_244639_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_244639'>安得<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_12_244639", 244639, "Clauses/24/Comments/0")'>牙旷</span>手，提耳发其聪。<div id='poem_sentence_12_244639_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_244639'></div><div id='poem_sentence_13_244639_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_244534' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_244534' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_content_244534'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_244534'>幕府多俊良，乘间得邀命。<div id='poem_sentence_0_244534_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_244534'>陈觞四座合，清笑发高兴。<div id='poem_sentence_1_244534_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_244534'>冰梨走咸黾，霜橘荐穰邓。<div id='poem_sentence_2_244534_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_244534'>肴羞愧无珍，粗竭我家称。<div id='poem_sentence_3_244534_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_244534'>礼酬嫌已拘，戏罚甘太横。<div id='poem_sentence_4_244534_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_244534'>诗诵唐人为，议法汉儒正。<div id='poem_sentence_5_244534_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_244534'>新嘲时巧发，诡令或孤迸。<div id='poem_sentence_6_244534_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_244534'>聊矜一时快，岂校负与胜。<div id='poem_sentence_7_244534_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_244534'>行伤昆弟别，且乐宾友盛。<div id='poem_sentence_8_244534_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_244534'>但愿会合频，醉日敢辞并。<div id='poem_sentence_9_244534_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_244534'></div><div id='poem_sentence_10_244534_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_244520' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_244520' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/244520?labeling=true' target='_blank'>饮圣俞西轩</a><span class='authorDate'>（1046年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34428, "北宋", "韩维", "poem_title_244520")'>韩维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_244520_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_244520'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_244520'>欢常以饮合，欢意则非外。<div id='poem_sentence_0_244520_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_244520'>今吾二三子，共此西轩会。<div id='poem_sentence_1_244520_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_244520'>主人吾儒秀，言与二雅配。<div id='poem_sentence_2_244520_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_244520'>酒行倡大论，文字略琐碎。<div id='poem_sentence_3_244520_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_244520'>上言评人物，要当本诸内。<div id='poem_sentence_4_244520_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_244520'>下言讥为学，不以满自概。<div id='poem_sentence_5_244520_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_244520'>唐之众诗人，区别各异派。<div id='poem_sentence_6_244520_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_244520'>一经君子评，敛凿<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：音作。）</span>弃秕糒。<div id='poem_sentence_7_244520_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_244520'>予曰吾圣俞，名足通后代。<div id='poem_sentence_8_244520_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_244520'>答我文如韩，尚有六经在。<div id='poem_sentence_9_244520_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_244520'>况吾何所立，闻誉若抱趸。<div id='poem_sentence_10_244520_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_244520'>圣俞善诱掖，斯语不无戒。<div id='poem_sentence_11_244520_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_244520'>意欲令吾曹，事业进以大。<div id='poem_sentence_12_244520_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_244520'>我虽顽无能，闻此亦健快。<div id='poem_sentence_13_244520_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_244520'>呼觞满自引，不畏坐客怪。<div id='poem_sentence_14_244520_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_244520'>归来书短篇，聊以记所佩。<div id='poem_sentence_15_244520_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_244520'></div><div id='poem_sentence_16_244520_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1046&endYear=1046')">1046年</a>　拜访隐士孔旼。作品：《谒孔先生》《送孔先生还山》《下横岭望宁极社》<div id='poem_133146' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_133146' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/133146?labeling=true' target='_blank'>谒孔先生</a><span class='authorDate'>（1046年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34428, "北宋", "韩维", "poem_title_133146")'>韩维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_133146_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_133146'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_133146'>月出高树枝，影动酒樽处。<div id='poem_sentence_0_133146_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_133146'>树深月色薄，稍以灯火助。<div id='poem_sentence_1_133146_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_133146'>主人喜我过，斟酌亦云屡。<div id='poem_sentence_2_133146_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_133146'>于时幸无累，所谈非近务。<div id='poem_sentence_3_133146_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_133146'>凉风自远生，清景澹吾虑。<div id='poem_sentence_4_133146_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_133146'>方期西山秋，历览陪杖屦。<div id='poem_sentence_5_133146_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_133146'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_133146_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_244644' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_244644' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/244644?labeling=true' target='_blank'>送孔先生还山</a><span class='authorDate'>（1046年）</span><span class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_244644_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_244644'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_244644'>先生<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_0_244644", 244644, "Clauses/0/Comments/0")'>乐道</span>者，于世澹无欲。<div id='poem_sentence_0_244644_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_244644'>高风自绝人，正行不违俗。<div id='poem_sentence_1_244644_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_244644'>朅来城阙游，不受尘事触。<div id='poem_sentence_2_244644_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_244644'>目久望林壑，驾言反幽筑。<div id='poem_sentence_3_244644_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_244644'>家临滍水阳，路转春山曲。<div id='poem_sentence_4_244644_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_244644'>东风吹百花，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_5_244644", 244644, "Clauses/11/Comments/0")'>红紫</span>满岩谷。<div id='poem_sentence_5_244644_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_244644'>蚕桑事未起，<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_244644", 244644, "Clauses/13/Comments/0")'>农里</span>得<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_6_244644", 244644, "Clauses/13/Comments/1")'>徵逐</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_6_244644_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_244644_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_244644'>应念尘中人，胡为自羁跼。<div id='poem_sentence_9_244644_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1046&endYear=1046')">1046年</a>　是年冬,孙永路过颖桥,韩维从许昌到颖桥与孙永相聚,作诗记之。作品：《答曼叔见谢颖桥相过之什》《颖桥会曼叔坐中写呈》<div id='poem_244747' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_244747' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/244747?labeling=true' target='_blank'>答曼叔见谢颍桥相过之什<span class='inlineComment2'>（时宁极先生同往）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1046年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34428, "北宋", "韩维", "poem_title_244747")'>韩维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_244747_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_244747'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_244747'>颍川今古贤豪多，后生继者为谁何。<div id='poem_sentence_0_244747_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_244747'>吾交曼叔少挺出，力自树立非由它。<div id='poem_sentence_1_244747_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_244747'>潜心直欲到圣处，论议不避况与轲。<div id='poem_sentence_2_244747_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_244747'>读书下笔知所趣，崇树兰茝遗蒿莪。<div id='poem_sentence_3_244747_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_244747'>轩昂头角事高大，肯与世俗同其波。<div id='poem_sentence_4_244747_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_244747'>一从得官坐山县，有如鸷鸟著网罗。<div id='poem_sentence_5_244747_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_244747'>朝符暮檄困奔走，尚畏官长来<span class='link' id='poem_sentence_7_244747'>时时矫首尘埃下，窥睹风月偷吟哦。<div id='poem_sentence_7_244747_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_244747'>我怜轶才就羁绊，岁一往视无蹉跎。<div id='poem_sentence_8_244747_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_244747'>扁舟远放汝水岸，浊酒暮醉高阳阿。<div id='poem_sentence_9_244747_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_244747'>嘲俳乘醉忽以发，驶如凿水放九河。<div id='poem_sentence_17_244747_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_244747'>哀弦孤引四坐寂，继以<span class='link' class='poemContent' id='poem_content_244625'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_244625'>日月忽已远，再见新谷升。<div id='poem_sentence_0_244625_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_244625'>丧期有常数，吉我衣与襟。<div id='poem_sentence_1_244625_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_244625'>俯仰自悲咤，泪下肝胆崩。<div id='poem_sentence_2_244625_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_244625'>尚推立身报，未即泯馀生。<div id='poem_sentence_3_244625_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_244625'>肃肃忠宪公，秉德辅休明。<div id='poem_sentence_4_244625_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_244625'>报国有遗意，训言犹在听。<div id='poem_sentence_10_244625'>扫冢奉时祭，履田课春耕。<div id='poem_sentence_10_244625_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_244625'>既无公家责，聊徇狷者情。<div id='poem_sentence_4_244528'>野性不受羁，尘事忧见桎。<div id='poem_sentence_4_244528_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_244528'>况兹罹大艰，哀号重衰疾。<div id='poem_sentence_2_497547'>业履归舆议，铭文愧绝辞。<div id='poem_sentence_2_497547_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_497547'>沧浪亭下路，长负故人期<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_3_497547_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_497547'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_497547_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_497547'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_3_497547_0'>⑴ 自注：予与子美有沧浪之约，今则已矣。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_497547_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_497548' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_497548' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/497548?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其二 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1048年12月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_497548_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_497548'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_497548'>魄动书流怆<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>，诚通梦告悲<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_0_497548_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_497548'>人生要有尽，君没竟何施。<div id='poem_sentence_1_497548_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_497548'>白日空尘几，春风自酒卮。<div id='poem_sentence_2_497548_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_497548'>旅魂归未得，藁葬近要离。<div id='poem_sentence_3_497548_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_497548'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_497548_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_497548'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_0_497548_0'>⑴ 自注：子美去冬与余书云：藐无相见之期。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_0_497548_0'>⑵ 自注：余梦若有告子美亡者，旦而得讣音。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_497548_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_497549' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_497549' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/497549?labeling=true' target='_blank'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em'> 其三 </span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1048年12月）</span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言律诗</div></div><div id='poem_title_497549_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_497549'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_497549'>才大终为累，冤深岂复论。<div id='poem_sentence_0_497549_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_497549'>几年流落恨，千里寂寥魂。<div id='poem_sentence_1_497549_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_497549'>功业初怀负，风流秀句存。<div id='poem_sentence_2_497549_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_497549'>英灵邈无所，洒泪望阊门。<div id='poem_sentence_3_497549_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_497549'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_497549_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1048&endYear=1048')">1048年</a>　是年,韩维、韩绛与梅尧臣交游。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1049&endYear=1049')">1049年</a>　与晏殊有诗歌唱和。作品：《和晏相公西湖》《和晏相公湖上遇雨》<div id='poem_244588' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_244588' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/244588?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和晏相公湖上遇雨</a><span class='authorDate'>（1049年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34428, "北宋", "韩维", "poem_title_244588")'>韩维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_244588_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_244588'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_244588'>公堂日多暇，薄暮游清池。<div id='poem_sentence_0_244588_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_244588'>孤云从西来，若与云盖期。<div id='poem_sentence_1_244588_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_244588'>急雨乱荷芰，红绿左右披。<div id='poem_sentence_2_244588_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_244588'>沙禽带湿起，簇簇守前坻。<div id='poem_sentence_3_244588_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_244588'>烟树晦空曲，蝉声寂无遗。<div id='poem_sentence_4_244588_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_244588'>残炎一洗濯，霁影开林西。<div id='poem_sentence_5_244588_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_244588'>禽飞还清波，蝉噪复故枝。<div id='poem_sentence_6_244588_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_244588'>晚槿扬朱华，秋草含碧滋。<div id='poem_sentence_7_244588_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_244588'>篙舟出堤去，微风满平猗。<div id='poem_sentence_8_244588_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_244588'>卷幔极长望，止见隗与箕。<div id='poem_sentence_9_244588_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_244588'>举酒无尘情，慨然起遐思。<div id='poem_sentence_10_244588_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_244588'>永怀古先训，默蹈通介宜。<div id='poem_sentence_11_244588_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_244588'>乃知贤哲心，所得非游嬉。<div id='poem_sentence_12_244588_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_244588'></div><div id='poem_sentence_13_244588_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1050&endYear=1050')">1050年</a><br /></div><div class='label1' id='bb9472a7db08468698ff10548908d3fb_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("bb9472a7db08468698ff10548908d3fb");'><span id='bb9472a7db08468698ff10548908d3fb_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1071&endYear=1071')">1071年</a>，55岁</div><div id='bb9472a7db08468698ff10548908d3fb' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1071&endYear=1071')">1071年5月</a>　初帝欲命韩维为御史中丞,韩维以兄韩绛居政府,力辞。遂出知襄州，改许州。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='eef84a47698d42ba88dcd500907ee5ef_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("eef84a47698d42ba88dcd500907ee5ef");'><span id='eef84a47698d42ba88dcd500907ee5ef_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1082&endYear=1083')">1082-1083年</a>，66-67岁</div><div id='eef84a47698d42ba88dcd500907ee5ef' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1082&endYear=1082')">1082年8月</a>　知颖昌府。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1083&endYear=1083')">1083年</a>　提举崇福宫。数引疾求罢,於是从其请。作品：《偃仰》<div id='poem_244681' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_244681' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/244681?labeling=true' target='_blank'>偃仰</a><span class='authorDate'>（1083年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34428, "北宋", "韩维", "poem_title_244681")'>韩维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_244681_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_244681'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_244681'>鹊噪庭柏喧，朝光来入隙。<div id='poem_sentence_0_244681_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_244681'>祠官谢馀事，偃仰百骸适。<div id='poem_sentence_1_244681_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_244681'>回思朝市人，小大各有役。<div id='poem_sentence_2_244681_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_244681'>区区就终尽，万古同一迹。<div id='poem_sentence_3_244681_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_244681'>而我遂慵散，兴味良不极。<div id='poem_sentence_4_244681_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_244681'>富贵非所慕，兹愿傥有获。<div id='poem_sentence_5_244681_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_244681'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_244681_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1083&endYear=1083')">1083年6月</a>　富弼卒,韩维为其撰写墓志铭。作品：《富文忠公墓志铭》<div id='poem_1169177' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169177' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169177?labeling=true' target='_blank'>富文忠公墓志铭</a><span class='authorDate'>（1083年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34428, "北宋", "韩维", "poem_title_1169177")'>韩维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169177_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169177'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169177'>元丰六年闰六月丙申，司徒韩国公致仕富公薨于京西里第之正寝，享年八十。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169177_comment'></div>天子闻讣震悼，为辍视朝，内出祭文，遣中贵人致祭，所以赙恤其家甚厚，且赠太尉、郑国公，谥曰文忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169177_comment'></div>公讳弼，字彦国，河南人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169177_comment'></div>曾大父内黄县令讳处谦，大父商州马步使讳令荀，考尚书都官员外郎讳言，并以公贵，赠中书令、尚书令，封邓、韩、秦三国为公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169177_comment'></div>曾祖母刘氏，祖母赵氏，母韩氏，赠鲁、韩、秦三国太夫人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169177_comment'></div>公少有大志，自刻苦为学，寓于僧坊，夜分略假寐凭几，既寤，则以冰雪沃面，复起读书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169177_comment'></div>应举京师，范文正公一见奇之，与语终日，曰：「真是王佐才也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169177_comment'></div>天圣八年，中茂才异等科，授将作监，出知河南府长水县。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169177_comment'></div>逾月，用李文定公辟，签书河阳节度判官厅公事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1169177_comment'></div>丁秦国公忧，服除，会范文正公言郭后不当废，左迁知睦州，公上疏曰：「废后非治世所宜，又以谏诤斥逐忠良，是一举而二失也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1169177_comment'></div>且国家缓急，何由得忠臣之心，来谏诤之论哉」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1169177_comment'></div>降通判绛州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1169177_comment'></div>景祐四年，召试馆职，擢太子中允，直集贤院。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1169177_comment'></div>从王沂公辟，通判郓州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1169177_comment'></div>宝元元年，赵元昊反，僭大号，朝廷仓卒措事，用人多失其当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1169177_comment'></div>公上疏陈八事：一曰宜先斩其使，以张国威，折奸谋；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1169177_comment'></div>二曰阅兵四方，使者旁午，非□□重威安民；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1169177_comment'></div>三曰兵兴，用度益广，宜佐以内府金帛，不宜专责外计，恐其乘急赋调，重伤民力；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1169177_comment'></div>四曰宜重赏战功，以劝死事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1169177_comment'></div>五曰不宜以厚禄高爵购募首恶，恐非示武明罚之道；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1169177_comment'></div>六曰不可用夏守赟充枢密使，以轻兵本，妨贤路；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1169177_comment'></div>七曰造次乏人，宜选群臣，不限资格，各举其类，以备任使；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1169177_comment'></div>八曰每遣边臣，请先赐对以观其才，抚以恩信，俾效死力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1169177_comment'></div>三年，召为开封府推官，赐五品服，兼知谏院。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1169177_comment'></div>时朝廷悉兵备西北，而东南九道俱无守卫，公请于每道要郡各募兵数千，部署训练，可以备他虞；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1169177_comment'></div>又茶盐之榷，利厚而法重，贫民误犯罪者众，愿省赢兵，节冗费，以佐国用而弛其税，以追王风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1169177_comment'></div>康定元年日食岁旦，公请罢宴彻乐以答天戒，戎使止就馆赐饮食，而不乐不宴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1169177_comment'></div>且曰：「万一北虏行之，则中国可愧矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1169177_comment'></div>后使北虏，归言：「虏果罢宴」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1169177_comment'></div>先是，执政者恶上闻其过失，因贬逐言者，遂榜朝堂，禁臣僚越职言事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1169177_comment'></div>公因日食上疏曰：「脩省之道，莫若通言路，使人各得陈上之得失，择善而行，则万务皆举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1169177_comment'></div>愿降诏求直言，革除越职之禁，则可以尽人情，答天意」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1169177_comment'></div>寻诏许臣下皆得言事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1169177_comment'></div>公又言：「奏封事者众，乞选侍臣分阅，择可用施行之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1169177_comment'></div>刘平战没，中贵人黄德和上章诬平以降贼，朝廷以兵禁守平家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1169177_comment'></div>公言：「中贵传命，平即日引道，志在忘家徇国，宁有降贼事？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1169177_comment'></div>此必德和败归，搆此语求自脱耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1169177_comment'></div>兼闻遣内侍往勘，深恐同类傅致，误朝廷赏罚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1169177_comment'></div>愿更遣文武谨信者以往」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1169177_comment'></div>后刘平果非降贼，德和坐腰斩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1169177_comment'></div>入内都知王守忠除陕西兵马都钤辖，公又言：「有唐之世，上始疑将帅，遂以内臣监军，取败非一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1169177_comment'></div>今命守忠为都钤辖，乃监军之任也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1169177_comment'></div>臣恐将权遂移，边将自此无功矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1169177_comment'></div>朝廷为罢守忠不遣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1169177_comment'></div>又言：「边事系国安危，不当专委枢密院而宰相不与。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1169177_comment'></div>乞如国初，令宰相兼枢密使」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1169177_comment'></div>西夏首领吹同乞砂、吹同山乞各称伪将相来降，朝廷补乞砂以奉职、山乞以借职安置，戍之荆、湖间。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1169177_comment'></div>公又言：「二人向化而来，其家必尽种族。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1169177_comment'></div>臣谓当厚加赏劳，访索敌情，以助破敌之计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1169177_comment'></div>今乃投之远方，待以羁囚，将何以怀劝来者」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1169177_comment'></div>又言：「朝廷取人路狭，所得文士而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1169177_comment'></div>天下多遗佚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1169177_comment'></div>愿以临难不顾，武勇绝伦，智足安边，才任将帅，谋虑宏远，可使绝域之类，多设科目，委诸路监司察举，以尽人才」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1169177_comment'></div>皆见施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1169177_comment'></div>明年，充三司盐铁判官，迁太常丞、史馆修撰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1169177_comment'></div>五月，改右正言、知制诰，纪察在京刑狱，赐三品服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_55_1169177_comment'></div>时有用伪祠部牒为僧者，事觉，牒乃堂吏所为，开封府狱具而不及堂吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_56_1169177_comment'></div>公白执政，请收伪造者付吏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_57_1169177_comment'></div>执政指其座曰：「他日公自当居此，奚事沽激为」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_58_1169177_comment'></div>公正色曰：「某以公事来察，何以甘言见诱邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_59_1169177_comment'></div>必得吏正其罪乃已」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_60_1169177_comment'></div>差同判太常寺，兼礼仪事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_61_1169177_comment'></div>时西陲困于用兵，庆历二年正月，北虏乘我间，聚其众境上，遣使萧英、刘六符来求地，朝廷以为忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_62_1169177_comment'></div>历选近臣任使事者，往往怯懦不肯行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_63_1169177_comment'></div>执政以公名闻，仁宗召对，面谕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_64_1169177_comment'></div>公曰：「主忧臣辱，今北虏狂慢如此，臣何敢自爱，以忧吾君」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_65_1169177_comment'></div>上先命公为接伴，以观其意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_66_1169177_comment'></div>英等入境，遣中使慰劳，英称足疾不拜，公谓曰：「仆尝使北，病卧车中，闻命尚起拜，今君岂得闻天子命而不拜」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_67_1169177_comment'></div>萧英惕然起，遂使人掖而拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_68_1169177_comment'></div>至大名尹觞，六符辞，公劝之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_69_1169177_comment'></div>六符曰：「在途久荷庇护，今日功亏一篑矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_70_1169177_comment'></div>公曰：「九仞之功已大，岂以一篑之微而遽弃邪」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_71_1169177_comment'></div>六符遂尽觞，退谓公曰：「九仞之言甚善，愿卒成之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_72_1169177_comment'></div>公曰：「敢不奉教」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_73_1169177_comment'></div>自是英等始开口论议，公亦推诚心与之往复，因尽得其所以来之状上闻，且请遣大臣至馆议所欲与。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_74_1169177_comment'></div>仁宗遣御史中丞贾文元为馆伴议之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_75_1169177_comment'></div>初，敌欲得晋祖所与关南十县者，朝廷不许；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_76_1169177_comment'></div>而议欲结婚，以宗室允宁女嫁其子梁王；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_77_1169177_comment'></div>或增岁遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_78_1169177_comment'></div>公闻之，谓所亲曰：「北虏无名肆慢，不得已者，可少增岁币，奈何以婚姻许之」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_79_1169177_comment'></div>四月，除枢密直学士，辞不受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_80_1169177_comment'></div>寻假资政殿学士、尚书户部侍郎使契丹。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_81_1169177_comment'></div>至虏帐，其馆伴刘六符曰：「公来，得非以结婚与岁遗事邪」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_82_1169177_comment'></div>公曰：「然」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_83_1169177_comment'></div>六符曰：「北朝皇帝坚欲割地，亦尝议及之乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_84_1169177_comment'></div>公曰：「北朝若欲割地，此必志在败盟，假此为名。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_85_1169177_comment'></div>南朝决不从，有横戈相待耳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_86_1169177_comment'></div>六符曰：「若两朝坚执，则事安得济」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_87_1169177_comment'></div>公曰：「北朝无故求地，南朝不即发兵拒却，而遣使好词更议，嫁女、益岁币，犹不从，乃是北朝坚执，非南朝执也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_88_1169177_comment'></div>及见虏主，公曰：「两朝人主父子继好垂四十年，一旦忽求割地，不知何故？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_89_1169177_comment'></div>两主无由相见，故遣愚臣问其所以」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_90_1169177_comment'></div>虏主曰：「南朝违约，塞雁门，又河北展塘水，治城隍，点民兵，将以何为？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_91_1169177_comment'></div>诸臣竞请兴兵，寡人谓不若遣使求关南故地，求而不得，兴兵未晚」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_92_1169177_comment'></div>公对曰：「雁门近元昊境，虑其潜有浸轶，故塞之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_93_1169177_comment'></div>塘水成于何承矩，事在通好前，以地卑水聚，故滋广耳；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_94_1169177_comment'></div>城隍完葺其旧，民兵按故籍补之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_95_1169177_comment'></div>皆非创有增立也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_96_1169177_comment'></div>虏主曰：「微卿言，不知其详」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_97_1169177_comment'></div>又曰：「朕欲得者祖宗故地」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_98_1169177_comment'></div>公曰：「晋高祖以卢龙一道赂契丹，周世宗复取关南，皆异代事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_99_1169177_comment'></div>宋兴已九十年，岂得复理前代所取之地乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_100_1169177_comment'></div>必欲各理旧疆，恐非北朝之利也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_101_1169177_comment'></div>虏主无言，徐曰：「元昊称藩尚主，南朝加兵，独不先告我，何也」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_102_1169177_comment'></div>公曰：「北朝向伐高丽、黑水，岂尝报朝廷乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_103_1169177_comment'></div>兼天子遣臣致意于陛下曰：『向不知元昊与弟国通姻，以其负恩扰边，故加讨戮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_104_1169177_comment'></div>而弟有烦言，击之则伤兄弟之情，不击则不忍坐视吏民之死而莫救也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_105_1169177_comment'></div>不知弟何以处之』」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_106_1169177_comment'></div>虏主顾其臣胡语良久，曰：「元昊为寇，岂有使南朝不击之理」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_107_1169177_comment'></div>他日，六符谓公曰：「昔南朝太宗皇帝既平河东，遂袭幽燕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_108_1169177_comment'></div>今虽云西边用兵，无乃复欲窥幽蓟乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_109_1169177_comment'></div>公曰：「其时北朝先遣拽刺梅里来聘问，而复出兵石岭关以助河东。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_110_1169177_comment'></div>太宗怒其反覆，故伐燕蓟，盖北朝自取之也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_111_1169177_comment'></div>六符又曰：「吾主不受金帛，坚欲十县，如何」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_112_1169177_comment'></div>公曰：「南朝皇帝曾言：『凡为人子孙，岂敢妄以祖宗土地与人？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_113_1169177_comment'></div>昔澶渊之役，盟约相好，章圣尚不与昭圣关南县，岂今日而反求多邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_114_1169177_comment'></div>且北朝要十县，不过利其租赋耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_115_1169177_comment'></div>今以金帛代之，亦足坐资国用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_116_1169177_comment'></div>朕念两国生民，不忍使之肝脑涂地，不爱金帛，屈己以徇北朝之欲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_117_1169177_comment'></div>亲如家人，兄顺其弟，弟亦顺兄，则睦矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_118_1169177_comment'></div>兄既顺弟，而弟不顺兄，则必致争阋。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_119_1169177_comment'></div>若北朝必欲得地，是志在背盟弃好，朕独得避用兵乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_120_1169177_comment'></div>且澶渊之盟，天地神祇，实共临之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_121_1169177_comment'></div>今北朝先发兵端，朕不愧于心，亦不愧于天地神祇矣』」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_122_1169177_comment'></div>六符谓其介曰：「南朝皇帝存心如此大善，当共奏使两主意通」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_123_1169177_comment'></div>翌日，召公同猎，引公马自近，问所欲言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_124_1169177_comment'></div>公曰：「南朝唯欲欢好之久耳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_125_1169177_comment'></div>虏主曰：「我得地则欢好可久」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_126_1169177_comment'></div>公曰：「南朝皇帝遣臣闻于陛下：『北朝若欲得祖宗故地，南朝亦岂肯失祖宗故地邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_127_1169177_comment'></div>且北朝既以得地为荣，则南朝亦以失地为辱矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_128_1169177_comment'></div>兄弟之国，岂可使一荣一辱？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_129_1169177_comment'></div>朕非忘燕蓟旧封，亦安可复理此事？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_130_1169177_comment'></div>正应彼此自谕耳』」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_131_1169177_comment'></div>退而六符告公曰：「皇帝闻公『荣辱』之言，意甚悟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_132_1169177_comment'></div>然金帛坚不欲取，唯结婚可议耳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_133_1169177_comment'></div>公曰：「结婚易生衅隙，盖夫妇情好难必兼，人命脩短或异，则所盟不终，不若增金帛之便也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_134_1169177_comment'></div>六符曰：「南朝皇帝向自有言」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_135_1169177_comment'></div>公曰：「帝女才四岁，成婚须在十馀年后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_136_1169177_comment'></div>虽选宗女成婚，亦须四五年后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_137_1169177_comment'></div>今欲释目前之疑，岂能待哉」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_138_1169177_comment'></div>公又揣虏欲结婚意在多得金币，因曰：「南朝嫁长公主，故事，资从不过十万缗耳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_139_1169177_comment'></div>由是虏缓结婚之意，且谕公归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_140_1169177_comment'></div>公曰：「二论未决，何敢便还？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_141_1169177_comment'></div>愿留毕议」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_142_1169177_comment'></div>虏主曰：「候卿再来，当择一事受之，宜以誓书俱至也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_143_1169177_comment'></div>公乃还奏，仁宗悦，除吏部郎中、枢密直学士，又以辞不受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_144_1169177_comment'></div>七月，复假前官议前事以往，受书并口传之词于政府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_145_1169177_comment'></div>公既行至灵寿，独念未尝见国书，其中或有与口传违异，则无以折敌示信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_146_1169177_comment'></div>乃发书视之，果不同。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_147_1169177_comment'></div>遂疾驰复至京师，日欲晡矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_148_1169177_comment'></div>径叩閤门求对，因宿侍宿舍一夕，易书而行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_149_1169177_comment'></div>至其国，虏主曰：「寡人熟思卿前言，诚不如金帛便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_150_1169177_comment'></div>然受之无名，须于书中加一『献』字乃可」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_151_1169177_comment'></div>公曰：「『献』字乃下奉上之辞，非可施于敌国。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_152_1169177_comment'></div>况南朝为兄，岂有兄献于弟乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_153_1169177_comment'></div>虏主曰：「南朝以厚币遗我，是惧我也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_154_1169177_comment'></div>『献』字何可惜」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_155_1169177_comment'></div>公曰：「南朝皇帝守祖宗之土宇，继先皇之盟好，以善意相承，故致币帛以代干戈，盖生灵是恤，岂惧北朝哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_156_1169177_comment'></div>今陛下忽发此言，正欲绝弃旧好，以必不可之势相要耳，则南朝亦何暇顾生灵哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_157_1169177_comment'></div>虏主曰：「改为『纳』字如何」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_158_1169177_comment'></div>公曰：「亦不可」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_159_1169177_comment'></div>虏主曰：「卿无固执，恐败乃主事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_160_1169177_comment'></div>我若拥兵南下，岂不祸乃国耶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_161_1169177_comment'></div>公曰：「陛下出兵，能保其必胜否」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_162_1169177_comment'></div>虏主曰：「不能」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_163_1169177_comment'></div>公曰：「胜既不保，安知其不败耶」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_164_1169177_comment'></div>虏主曰：「南朝既以金币与我，『纳』字何惜？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_165_1169177_comment'></div>况自古有之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_166_1169177_comment'></div>公曰：「自古惟唐高祖臣事突厥而借兵焉，当时赂遗，或称『纳』，今则不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_167_1169177_comment'></div>况其后颉利为太宗所擒，岂复更有是理」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_168_1169177_comment'></div>虏主默然，见公词色俱厉，度不可夺，曰：「我别遣使与南朝皇帝议之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_169_1169177_comment'></div>公自至虏中，日与其君臣论难，或自旦及夕，至指帐前高山曰：「此尚可踰，若欲『献』、『纳』二字，则如天不可得而上也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_170_1169177_comment'></div>使臣头可断，此议决不可诺」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_171_1169177_comment'></div>于是，虏留所许岁增金帛誓书，复遣耶律仁先、刘六符赍其国誓书以来，仍求『纳』字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_172_1169177_comment'></div>公至都，言曰：「契丹求『献』、『纳』二字甚急，臣既以死拒之矣，愿朝廷终绝之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_173_1169177_comment'></div>公初奉使，闻一女卒，再奉使，闻一男生，皆不顾，亟行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_174_1169177_comment'></div>寻迁翰林学士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_175_1169177_comment'></div>公上章及面启曰：「朝廷方事西路，河北无备，臣奉使所以不敢死争者，实虑兴戎以败国事，功于何有而遽受赏哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_176_1169177_comment'></div>愿陛下增修武备，俟衅而动，以洗国耻」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_177_1169177_comment'></div>卒不拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_178_1169177_comment'></div>仁宗益嘉公劳而不有，三年三月，遂命公为枢密副使，辞不受，拜资政殿学士，兼翰林院侍读学士，知审官院。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_179_1169177_comment'></div>七月，再除枢密副使，固辞不受，至持诰命纳于上前而罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_180_1169177_comment'></div>逾月，复除前命，值元昊使人致辞，群臣班于紫宸殿门，有诏促公假枢密院班，方御殿，且命宰相谕旨曰：「朝廷用贤，不缘使虏之劳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_181_1169177_comment'></div>公知不可辞，方受拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_182_1169177_comment'></div>公既典几密，自以为遭时得位，知无不为。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_183_1169177_comment'></div>时晏元献公为宰相，范文正公参知政事，杜祁公居枢密，公与之同心合力，期致太平。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_184_1169177_comment'></div>仁宗开龙图、天章阁，命辅臣各条天下大事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_185_1169177_comment'></div>公列上十馀事及河北安边十三策，又乞择宗室之才者试以为政，渐壮藩屏，又言：「安民在守宰，请令二府合议，择诸路转运使，转运使择知州，知州择知县，则天下得人矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_186_1169177_comment'></div>元昊遣使奉书称「男兀卒曩霄上父皇帝」，而不称臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_187_1169177_comment'></div>公又言：「事在慎始，向闻西路待其使过厚，又听其称伪官，入见赐与亦加多，此适足以张其骄慢之心耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_188_1169177_comment'></div>且曩霄尚臣属契丹，奈何后中国乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_189_1169177_comment'></div>由是朝廷却其使，卒令称臣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_190_1169177_comment'></div>四年七月，契丹来告举兵讨元昊。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_191_1169177_comment'></div>十二月，朝廷册元昊为夏国主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_192_1169177_comment'></div>使将行复止，以俟虏使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_193_1169177_comment'></div>公又言：「虏使未至而行，则事由我出；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_194_1169177_comment'></div>使至而后行，则恩归契丹矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_195_1169177_comment'></div>遂遣使行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_196_1169177_comment'></div>契丹发兵，会元昊讨呆儿族，道出河东境外。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_197_1169177_comment'></div>仁宗面谕辅臣：「宜设备待之」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_198_1169177_comment'></div>公发九事，料其必不入寇，已而果然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_199_1169177_comment'></div>时天下久安，事或靡敝不振。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_200_1169177_comment'></div>京师要司厚廪多近倖领之，至有十年不代者，公为立三岁之任；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_201_1169177_comment'></div>州县官吏偷惰不举职，置按察使以纠之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_202_1169177_comment'></div>中外多不便公者，会大臣亦有以飞语中公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_203_1169177_comment'></div>仁宗虽不听，而公惧不自安，因保州贼平，求为河北路宣抚使以避之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_204_1169177_comment'></div>使还，道除资政殿学士知郓州，兼京东西路安抚使，寻又罢公安抚使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_205_1169177_comment'></div>后岁馀，谗言不验，加给事中，移知青州，兼京东东路安抚使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_206_1169177_comment'></div>河北大水，流民入京东者不可胜数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_207_1169177_comment'></div>公择所部丰稔者五州，劝民出粟，随在所贮之，以助赈给。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_208_1169177_comment'></div>行于乡村城郭，得庐舍可以寓人者十馀万所。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_209_1169177_comment'></div>官吏自前资待问寄居者，各给以俸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_210_1169177_comment'></div>即民所聚，别其老幼病瘠者，籍名授券，分主而均廪之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_211_1169177_comment'></div>下至器用薪刍微细之物，处之皆有法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_212_1169177_comment'></div>不幸死者，即为收瘗，公自为文祭之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_213_1169177_comment'></div>其明年夏麦既登，乃为计其道里远近，俾裹囊遣归业所，全活者五十万人，募而为兵者又万馀人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_214_1169177_comment'></div>天子闻之，遣使劳公，即拜礼部侍郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_215_1169177_comment'></div>公曰：「恤灾赈乏，职也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_216_1169177_comment'></div>辞不受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_217_1169177_comment'></div>王则据贝州叛，齐之禁兵密谋，于时屠其城以应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_218_1169177_comment'></div>有告变者，公以齐非所部，且虑事泄变作，会中使张从训衔命在青州，公檄从训会齐官吏捕之，悉从擒戮，而自劾擅遣中使之罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_219_1169177_comment'></div>仁宗嘉之，再除礼部侍郎，公又恳辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_220_1169177_comment'></div>俄迁资政殿大学士，未几，又拜礼部侍郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_221_1169177_comment'></div>以秦国太夫人久去乡里，求徙京西。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_222_1169177_comment'></div>移知郑州，又移蔡州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_223_1169177_comment'></div>加观文殿大学士，知河阳，迁户部侍郎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_224_1169177_comment'></div>至和二年，拜宣徽南院使，判并州，兼河东路经略安抚使。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_225_1169177_comment'></div>六月，拜同中书门下平章事，集贤殿大学士，与文潞公同日宣制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_226_1169177_comment'></div>仁宗遣小黄门数辈觇于廷，士大夫皆以得人相庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_227_1169177_comment'></div>后数日，翰林欧阳公入对。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_228_1169177_comment'></div>仁宗曰：「近除文彦博、富弼作宰相，士人相贺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_229_1169177_comment'></div>古人求相，或得之梦卜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_230_1169177_comment'></div>今朕得于人情，何待梦卜也」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_231_1169177_comment'></div>欧阳公顿首称贺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_232_1169177_comment'></div>嘉祐初，仁宗弗豫，不御殿者久之，虽执政不得许知其起居状。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_233_1169177_comment'></div>公与文潞公率辅臣求入侍疾，内侍都知止之曰：「未有诏旨」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_234_1169177_comment'></div>公叱曰：「岂有宰相一月而不见天子乎」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_235_1169177_comment'></div>径入见上，因请以监视祷禳留宿殿中。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_236_1169177_comment'></div>自是宫掖事无巨细皆白宰相而后敢行，中外晏然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_237_1169177_comment'></div>仁宗春秋渐高，国嗣未立，公与同列议择宗室之贤者以建储贰，遂以英宗名上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_238_1169177_comment'></div>仁宗曰：「朕志已定，卿等勿疑也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_239_1169177_comment'></div>三年，加礼部尚书，昭文馆大学士，监修国史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_240_1169177_comment'></div>时仁宗倦勤，庶政皆仰成宰相。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_241_1169177_comment'></div>公以州县繇役赋敛或非法制，乃选使分行诸道，命之曰「宽恤民力」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_242_1169177_comment'></div>多所釐正，人赖其泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_243_1169177_comment'></div>又弛茶禁，通商贩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_244_1169177_comment'></div>民以不犯法，刑为之省。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_245_1169177_comment'></div>五年，丁秦国太夫人忧，诏特罢春宴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_246_1169177_comment'></div>五遣中使起公复位，公恳求终丧，从之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_247_1169177_comment'></div>仍给半俸，辞不受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_248_1169177_comment'></div>英宗即位，公服除，拜枢密使、同中书门下平章事，迁户部尚书。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_249_1169177_comment'></div>踰年，以足疾求解机务，章二十上，拜镇海军节度使、同中书门下平章事，判河阳，封祁国公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_250_1169177_comment'></div>今上践祚，移镇武宁军，进封郑国公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_251_1169177_comment'></div>屡乞罢将相任，上以公累朝辅佐，年耆德盛，尤虚心待之，以尚书左仆射、观文殿大学士、集禧观使召公，公以足疾未任拜，固辞，诏以新官复判河阳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_252_1169177_comment'></div>熙宁元年正月，徙判汝州，且俾入觐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_253_1169177_comment'></div>以公足疾许肩舆至崇政殿门，令男绍隆扶掖以进，且命不拜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_254_1169177_comment'></div>又以门距殿远，更御内东门便殿见之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_255_1169177_comment'></div>赐坐从容，日昃始退。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_256_1169177_comment'></div>仍赐其子绯衣银鱼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_257_1169177_comment'></div>盖近世宠遇大臣，未有恩礼如此之厚也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_258_1169177_comment'></div>上欲复以集禧观使留之，公恳辞，之镇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_259_1169177_comment'></div>明年正月，再召赴阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_260_1169177_comment'></div>上之将召之，先遣中使谕之曰：「卿今兹毋得重辞，当力疾入辅，为宗社计」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_261_1169177_comment'></div>二月，遂除司空，兼侍郎、昭文馆大学士，赐甲第一区，皆不受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_262_1169177_comment'></div>复拜左仆射、门下侍郎、同平章事，未陛见，会有以「灾异皆常数，不系人事得失」言于上前者，公上章曰：「《春秋》书灾异，所以警悟人君，使恐惧修省。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_263_1169177_comment'></div>《洪范》庶徵，亦以五事而致，未闻归之天数也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_264_1169177_comment'></div>陛下万一过听，寅畏消复之意有时而怠，则亏损圣德，无甚于此」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_265_1169177_comment'></div>是时，群臣请上尊号及听乐，上以久旱不许，而群臣尤固请听乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_266_1169177_comment'></div>公又言：「故事，有灾变皆彻乐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_267_1169177_comment'></div>恐陛下以同天节契丹使与群臣当上寿，故未断其来请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_268_1169177_comment'></div>臣以为陛下始亲庶政，四海属耳目，尤宜日新盛业，以示四邻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_269_1169177_comment'></div>愿并上寿罢之，益见陛下严恭天戒之美」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_270_1169177_comment'></div>从之，即日而雨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_271_1169177_comment'></div>公又言：「陛下答谢天戒不为不至，上天报应不为不速。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_272_1169177_comment'></div>愿陛下不以今日得雨为喜，更以累年灾变为惧，远离奸幸，亲近忠良，恭畏上天，则太平可致」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_273_1169177_comment'></div>上亲书答诏曰：「义忠言亲，理正文直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_274_1169177_comment'></div>茍非意在爱君，志存王室，何以臻此！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_275_1169177_comment'></div>敢不置之枕席，铭之肺腑，终老是戒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_276_1169177_comment'></div>更愿公自兹输诚翊辅，则天灾不难弭，太平可立俟也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_277_1169177_comment'></div>公又陈：「君子小人情伪系王道之消长，天下之安危，望陛下深加辨察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_278_1169177_comment'></div>所喜者不可遽用，所怒者不可遽弃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_279_1169177_comment'></div>用舍小失，则招致祸败不细矣」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_280_1169177_comment'></div>八月，以疾辞位，拜武宁军节度使、同中书门下平章事，判河南府。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_281_1169177_comment'></div>复用公请，改判亳州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_282_1169177_comment'></div>四年，提举河南常平仓赵济，言公于青苗法不行，除左仆射，判汝州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_283_1169177_comment'></div>再上章愿归洛养疾，许之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_284_1169177_comment'></div>其年冬，请老，拜司空，复武宁节，兼同中书门下平章事，进封韩国公致仕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_285_1169177_comment'></div>元丰三年，官制改，授开府仪同三司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_286_1169177_comment'></div>又以王同老言嘉祐中其父尝与启建储事，上嘉公初不自言，特拜司徒，仍以其子绍京为阁门祗候。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_287_1169177_comment'></div>公为人端厚沈正，临事而慎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_288_1169177_comment'></div>其处己谋国必熟复周虑，度不万全不发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_289_1169177_comment'></div>接士大夫，尽诚以有礼，虽布衣必与之亢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_290_1169177_comment'></div>不妄笑语以下宾客，为声名，嘉善嫉邪，出于天性。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_291_1169177_comment'></div>居閒，犹询问当世人物，以知其贤不肖，尤慎许与，未尝轻以加人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_292_1169177_comment'></div>出入尊宠垂四十年，而服用素约，无声色之玩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_293_1169177_comment'></div>虽高年，未尝一日废书不观，以至释氏、老庄方外之说，莫不究极精致。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_294_1169177_comment'></div>有文集八十卷，藏于家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_295_1169177_comment'></div>公尝语人曰：「吾才学非能过人，但有不欺耳」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_296_1169177_comment'></div>盖公之所以自养者如此，故其行己也，外如其中，其事君也，终如其初，久而益见信于天下，虽穷阎远国，莫不知公之姓与官号。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_297_1169177_comment'></div>北虏使每至，必候公出处，问其安否。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_298_1169177_comment'></div>公虽退居，明诏之所咨访，密章之所启告，盖不乏矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_299_1169177_comment'></div>至其将没，犹以遗稿一通付其子上之，然其详莫得而知也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_300_1169177_comment'></div>推公之意，茍可以益君上、厚民人者，盖忘其身之老且死而言之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_301_1169177_comment'></div>呜呼，可谓忠已！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_302_1169177_comment'></div>初，公之将生，秦国太夫人梦幡旗鹤雁甚众，降集其家，云天有赦，寤而生公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_303_1169177_comment'></div>其将薨，有大星殒于所居还政堂之后。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_304_1169177_comment'></div>噫！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_305_1169177_comment'></div>天之生大贤不数，生则必福其国，泽其民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_306_1169177_comment'></div>如公之为相，则首定储位，以启神圣，为社稷无疆之休；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_307_1169177_comment'></div>其奉使，则辨折强虏，攘其奸萌，易干戈为和好；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_308_1169177_comment'></div>其抚东夏，则安辑流冗，以食以处，续将绝之命者数十万人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_309_1169177_comment'></div>则其兆神灵之应，锡寿宠之享，固其理然，恶足怪哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_310_1169177_comment'></div>公之配曰周国夫人，晏氏元献公之女也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_311_1169177_comment'></div>贤静有法度，公以为「真吾匹」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_312_1169177_comment'></div>男子三人：曰绍庭，朝奉郎；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_313_1169177_comment'></div>曰绍京，供备库副使，后公一月卒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_314_1169177_comment'></div>曰绍隆，光禄寺丞，早卒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_315_1169177_comment'></div>女子四人：长适观文殿学士冯京，卒；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_316_1169177_comment'></div>又以其次继室，封延安郡夫人；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_317_1169177_comment'></div>次适宣德郎范大宗；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_318_1169177_comment'></div>次适霍邱县令范大圭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_319_1169177_comment'></div>孙男女各三人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_320_1169177_comment'></div>周国夫人与其孤遂以公薨之年冬十一月庚申，奉公之柩葬于河南府河南县金谷乡南张里，从秦国公之兆也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_321_1169177_comment'></div>谓某辱公之知实厚且久，以铭见属，义不得辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_322_1169177_comment'></div>铭曰：</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_323_1169177'>富氏之先，其尚莫穷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_323_1169177_comment'></div>辰见于周，仕而不逢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_324_1169177_comment'></div>时君弗察，以死偿忠。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_325_1169177_comment'></div>爰及后世，显莫如公。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_326_1169177_comment'></div>公之筮仕，遭我仁宗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_327_1169177_comment'></div>奋辞发策，厥问载鸿。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_328_1169177_comment'></div>遂司谏垣，达帝之聪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_329_1169177_comment'></div>朝对夕启，靡言不从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_330_1169177_comment'></div>左右王体，蔚然古风。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_331_1169177_comment'></div>乃奉使指，抗旃龙庭。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_332_1169177_comment'></div>扶义据正，折其奸萌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_333_1169177_comment'></div>守地息民，讫如初盟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_334_1169177_comment'></div>出抚东夏，水溢民流。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_335_1169177_comment'></div>峙粮授室，毕给其求。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_336_1169177_comment'></div>既安既饱，复其先畴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_337_1169177_comment'></div>凡公之为，主是归正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_338_1169177_comment'></div>有其害之，必攘必争。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_339_1169177_comment'></div>奸谋险言，以撼皇听，崎岖杌隉，卒莫能病。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_340_1169177_comment'></div>既极而通，惟诚之胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_341_1169177_comment'></div>爰命作相，付畀邦政。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_342_1169177_comment'></div>质于朝言，人用胥庆。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_343_1169177_comment'></div>匪梦匪卜，天子神圣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_344_1169177_comment'></div>嘉祐之末，主鬯虚位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_345_1169177_comment'></div>聿求宗藩，首定圣嗣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_346_1169177_comment'></div>繄公一言，万世之利。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_347_1169177_comment'></div>上眷旧德，恩无与二。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_348_1169177_comment'></div>义忠言亲，形于诏旨。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_349_1169177_comment'></div>辞隆即安，屏翰是寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_350_1169177_comment'></div>公拜稽首，谢不任事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_351_1169177_comment'></div>将旄相绂，归老于第。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_352_1169177_comment'></div>优游偃息，默与道会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_353_1169177_comment'></div>翛然一室，物莫奸志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_354_1169177_comment'></div>惟是报国，老而益厉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_355_1169177_comment'></div>忠规谠谋，没然后已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_356_1169177_comment'></div>昔周之宣，天锡良辅。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_357_1169177_comment'></div>赋政四方，阙衮是补。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_358_1169177_comment'></div>柔亦不茹，刚亦不吐。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_359_1169177_comment'></div>迹公猷为，实蹈其武。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_360_1169177_comment'></div>砻坚勒休，以志公墓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_361_1169177_comment'></div>亿万斯年，为宋山甫<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南阳集》卷二九。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_362_1169177_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_363_1169177'>非□□重威安：原阙，据明钞本补。</div><div id='poem_sentence_363_1169177_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='8dbfb914a97f496a9db82017fcdaf2a2_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("8dbfb914a97f496a9db82017fcdaf2a2");'><span id='8dbfb914a97f496a9db82017fcdaf2a2_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1089&endYear=1098')">1089-1098年</a>，73-82岁</div><div id='8dbfb914a97f496a9db82017fcdaf2a2' class='detail'><a href="javascript: href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1091&endYear=1091')">1091年6月</a>　上《乞止就本州推勘赵仁恕狱奏》<div id='poem_1169132' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169132' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169132?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞止就本州推勘赵仁恕狱奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（元祐六年六月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: id='poem_content_1169132'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169132'>此狱连逮三百数十人，今前勘可断者已决四十二人，馀人尚多。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169132_comment'></div>方此盛暑，若依朝旨移于亳州置狱，即地远冒暑，淹系可矜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169132_comment'></div>仁恕之妻子已病危笃。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169132_comment'></div>士人家尚尔，细民可知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169132_comment'></div>愿止就本州别推。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1169132_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1092&endYear=1092')">1092年3月</a>　为太子少傅致仕。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1092&endYear=1092')">1092年9月</a>　乞再免南郊陪位,从之。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1093&endYear=1096')">1093-1096年</a>　居乡？<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1097&endYear=1097')">1097年2月</a>　黜韩维以下三十一人轻重有差。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1097&endYear=1097')">1097年5月</a>　谪崇信军节度副使,均州安置。经三子求情，哲宗特许其回归故里。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1098&endYear=1098')">1098年5月</a>　以左朝议大夫致仕。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1098&endYear=1098')">1098年11月25日</a>　是年卒。<br /></div>

id='poem_sentence_0_244536_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_244536'>归来不作留滞叹，能出窈窕夸樽前。<div id='poem_sentence_1_244536_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_244536'>前时宾客会清夜，横笛裂玉吹孤圜。<div id='poem_sentence_2_244536_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_244536'>新声妙逐柔指变，馀响欻与高云连。<div id='poem_sentence_3_244536_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_244536'>悲风萧瑟四座耸，清笑自足遗拘挛。<div id='poem_sentence_4_244536_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_244536'>近闻有疾勿药喜，主人欲饮期数贤。<div id='poem_sentence_5_244536_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_244536'>气羸曲节宜少缓，体软舞态当益妍。<div id='poem_sentence_6_244536_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_244536'>人生行乐不可后，幸及华月秋娟娟。<div id='poem_sentence_7_244536_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1054&endYear=1054')">1054年12月</a>　韩维与韩绛、欧阳修、刘敞聚饮，有诗寄江休复。作品：《和永叔小饮怀同州江十学士》<div id='poem_244540' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_244540' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/244540?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和永叔小饮怀同州江十学士</a><span class='authorDate'>（1054年12月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34428, "北宋", "韩维", "poem_title_244540")'>韩维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_244540_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_244540'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_244540'>翰林文章伯，好古名一世。<div id='poem_sentence_0_244540_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_244540'>家无金璧储，所宝书与器。<div id='poem_sentence_1_244540_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_244540'>北堂冬日明，有朋联骑至。<div id='poem_sentence_2_244540_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_244540'>新樽布几案，二鼎屹先置。<div id='poem_sentence_3_244540_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_244540'>大鼎葛所铭，小鼎泽而粹。<div id='poem_sentence_4_244540_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_244540'>坐恐至神物，光怪发非次。<div id='poem_sentence_5_244540_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_244540'>群贤刻金石，墨本来四裔。<div id='poem_sentence_6_244540_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_244540'>纷穰罢卷轴，指擿辨分隶。<div id='poem_sentence_7_244540_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_244540'>其中石赞藏，家法非一二。<div id='poem_sentence_8_244540_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_244540'>精庄与飘逸，两自有馀意。<div id='poem_sentence_9_244540_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_244540'>兴来辄长歌，欢至遂沉醉。<div id='poem_sentence_10_244540_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_244540'>颜饥足箪瓢，韩饮尚文字。<div id='poem_sentence_11_244540_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_244540'>乃知内可乐，不必钟鼓贵。<div id='poem_sentence_12_244540_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_244540'>温温江冯翊，兹理久所诣。<div id='poem_sentence_13_244540_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_244540'>赋诗多雅言，嗜酒见<span class='link' id='poem_sentence_15_244540'>岁晏不在席，使我长叹喟。<div id='poem_sentence_15_244540_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_244540'></div><div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1055&endYear=1055')">1055年</a>　是年，晏殊卒，维作诗文祭之。作品：《阳翟祭晏元献公文》《出留守府之东游李相园赵令竹林观楚家桂树余去岁数从元献公为此行作三绝句以道悲枪之意》。《晏元献公挽辞三首》<div id='poem_1169182' class='_poem'><div class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34428, "北宋", "韩维", "poem_title_1169182")'>韩维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169182_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169182'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169182'>公之道德，与言与事，叠见歌颂，没而不废，非维闇薄，所敢褒纪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169182_comment'></div>独念晚进，辱公提携，脱略尊严，降接陋卑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169182_comment'></div>酬酢篇咏，从容燕嬉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169182_comment'></div>治学粲然，右有左宜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169182_comment'></div>启告诲谕，发于诚辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169182_comment'></div>岂敢失坠，天实为之！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169182_comment'></div>呜呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169182_comment'></div>去年之春，拜公洛土。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169182_comment'></div>昔旆旋西，今柩窆许。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1169182_comment'></div>谁谓哀乐，近在仰俯！<div class='inline'
