"poem_title_244541")'>韩维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_244541_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_244541'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_244541'>弱岁抱衰病，掩关卧园庐。<div id='poem_sentence_0_244541_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_244541'>端居寡人事，永日惟对书。<div id='poem_sentence_1_244541_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_244541'>得花辄手植，生草每自锄。<div id='poem_sentence_2_244541_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_244541'>最怜脩竹姿，擢干青玉如。<div id='poem_sentence_3_244541_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_244541'>添栽岁岁广，翠色满窗疏。<div id='poem_sentence_4_244541_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_244541'>起坐一堂内，乐此不愿馀。<div id='poem_sentence_5_244541_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_244541'>偶来从吏役，幽事日以疏。<div id='poem_sentence_6_244541_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_244541'>出门何所见，扰扰尘中车。<div id='poem_sentence_7_244541_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_244541'>素怀就湮没，有恨不可摅。<div id='poem_sentence_8_244541_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_244541'>尚念禄仕微，欲返复踌躇。<div id='poem_sentence_9_244541_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_244541'>高贤侍天陛，文章冠严徐。<div id='poem_sentence_10_244541_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_244541'>迹虽台省游，志慕江湖渔。<div id='poem_sentence_11_244541_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_244541'>凤皇览辉下，阿阁正其居。<div id='poem_sentence_12_244541_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_244541'>顾惟蒿艾翮，分甘侣田鴽。<div id='poem_sentence_13_244541_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_244541'>因诗益自警，庶不忘厥初。<div id='poem_sentence_14_244541_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_244541'></div><div id='poem_sentence_15_244541_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1056&endYear=1056')">1056年</a>　刘敞出使契归,韩维作《奉答原甫登契丹岭见寄》<div id='poem_244618' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_244618' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/244618?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉答原甫登契丹岭见寄<span class='inlineComment2'>（原甫假翰林学士以行）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1056年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34428, "北宋", "韩维", "poem_title_244618")'>韩维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_244618_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_244618'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_244618'>中原昔失御，幽冀不复华。<div id='poem_sentence_0_244618_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_244618'>我朝示仁抚，金币岁屡加。<div id='poem_sentence_1_244618_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_244618'>君恩谨宣道，使才慎推差。<div id='poem_sentence_2_244618_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_244618'>翰林承命行，驱驾绝漠沙。<div id='poem_sentence_3_244618_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_244618'>晨登寒山岭，回望万里家。<div id='poem_sentence_4_244618_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_244618'>劲风搜貂裘，严冰断马挝。<div id='poem_sentence_5_244618_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_244618'>乡心感归雁，塞泪零悲笳。<div id='poem_sentence_6_244618_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_244618'>慷慨属国节，迢递博望槎。<div id='poem_sentence_7_244618_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_244618'>幸古有此贤，庶足开颦嗟。<div id='poem_sentence_8_244618_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_244618'>晴阳展归旗，喜气日以嘉。<div id='poem_sentence_9_244618_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_244618'>入门解征衫，金樽滟流霞。<div id='poem_sentence_10_244618_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_244618'>哀弦间清唱，娇鬟蔚如鸦。<div id='poem_sentence_11_244618_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_244618'>一慰行役劳，期君柳初芽。<div id='poem_sentence_12_244618_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_244618'></div><div id='poem_sentence_13_244618_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1057&endYear=1057')">1057年</a><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1058&endYear=1058')">1058年4月</a>　刘敞作《郓州乐郊》诗一首,韩维有和诗。作品：《奉同原甫耶州乐郊》<div id='poem_244606' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_244606' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/244606?labeling=true' target='_blank'>奉同原甫郓州乐郊</a><span class='authorDate'>（1058年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34428, "北宋", "韩维", "poem_title_244606")'>韩维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_244606_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_244606'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_244606'>诗人歌乐郊，以政不以游。<div id='poem_sentence_0_244606_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_244606'>太守名是地，岂非为民谋。<div id='poem_sentence_1_244606_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_244606'>下车布条教，惠爱春风柔。<div id='poem_sentence_2_244606_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_244606'>丹笔平枉讼，赭衣息奸偷。<div id='poem_sentence_3_244606_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_244606'>政和岁亦丰，闾里舞且讴。<div id='poem_sentence_4_244606_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_244606'>及我闲暇时，驾言此淹留。<div id='poem_sentence_5_244606_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_244606'>杂花艳暄朝，翠竹鲜霜秋。<div id='poem_sentence_6_244606_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_244606'>有台下观渔，有堂前抗侯。<div id='poem_sentence_7_244606_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_244606'>觞斝既纷错，管鼓亦喧啾。<div id='poem_sentence_8_244606_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_244606'>都人从公来，小大毕休休。<div id='poem_sentence_9_244606_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_244606'>施设苟异此，且为民所仇。<div id='poem_sentence_10_244606_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_244606'>台高池益深，不若墟与丘。<div id='poem_sentence_11_244606_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_244606'>贤而后能乐，轲言良有由。<div id='poem_sentence_12_244606_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_244606'>聊书太守意，庶几来者求。<div id='poem_sentence_13_244606_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_244606'></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_244606_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1058&endYear=1058')">1058年10月</a>　与刘敞同游京师附近的会灵观。作品：《次韵和原甫游会灵观》<div id='poem_244480' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_244480' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/244480?labeling=true' target='_blank'>次韵和原甫游会灵观</a><span class='authorDate'>（1058年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34428, "北宋", "韩维", "poem_title_244480")'>韩维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_244480_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_244480'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_244480'>松乔去我久，高驾不可攀。<div id='poem_sentence_0_244480_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_244480'>何意尘外游，近在王城间。<div id='poem_sentence_1_244480_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_244480'>先帝昔临御，抱冲启玄关。<div id='poem_sentence_2_244480_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_244480'>营宫奉岳镇，缥缈当人寰。<div id='poem_sentence_3_244480_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_244480'>疏泉抗台殿，拟迹三神山。<div id='poem_sentence_4_244480_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_244480'>想像列仙下，半空来佩环。<div id='poem_sentence_5_244480_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_244480'>云车倏容与，旄节俨成班。<div id='poem_sentence_6_244480_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_244480'>翩翾万玉女，红颊翠羽鬟。<div id='poem_sentence_7_244480_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_244480'>世人那得见，石坛空自闲。<div id='poem_sentence_8_244480_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_244480'>伊予厌羁跼，酷甚负病瘝。<div id='poem_sentence_9_244480_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_244480'>兹行适所愿，帖若贾在阛。<div id='poem_sentence_10_244480_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_244480'>春风吹园桃，几日朱霞殷。<div id='poem_sentence_11_244480_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_244480'>寒碧竹间见，新黄柳际还。<div id='poem_sentence_12_244480_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_244480'>主人非素期，促具初无艰。<div id='poem_sentence_13_244480_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_244480'>抗侯角善手，持觞发欢颜。<div id='poem_sentence_14_244480_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_244480'>尚无形骸累，安问绂与纶。<div id='poem_sentence_15_244480_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_16_244480'>跋马兴不尽，东池水潺潺。<div id='poem_sentence_16_244480_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_17_244480'></div><div id='poem_sentence_17_244480_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1059&endYear=1059')">1059年4月</a>　司徒致仕陈执中卒，礼官韩维议其谥曰荣灵。作品：《赠太师兼侍中陈执中溢荣灵议》《论陈执中溢荣灵书》《论陈执中直降勅谥恭第一状》《论陈执中直降勅谥恭第二》<div id='poem_1169038' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169038' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169038?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赠太师兼侍中陈执中谥荣灵议</a><span class='authorDate'>（嘉祐四年四月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34428, "北宋", "韩维", "poem_title_1169038")'>韩维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169038_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169038'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169038'>执中幸得以公卿子遭世承平，因缘一时之言，遂至贵显。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169038_comment'></div>皇祐之末，天子之后宫之丧，问所以葬祭之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169038_comment'></div>执中位为上相，不能总率群司，考正仪典，以承答天问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169038_comment'></div>知治丧皇仪非嫔御之礼，追册位号于宫帏有嫌，建庙用乐踰祖宗旧制，执中白而行之，曾不愧惮，遂使圣朝大典著非礼之举，此不忠之大者！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169038_comment'></div>闺门之内，礼分不明，夫人正室疏薄自绌，庶妾贱人悍逸不制，丑声流布，行路共知，此又治家无足言者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169038_comment'></div>夫宰相所当秉道率礼以弼天子，正身齐家以议百官，执中不务出此，而方杜门深居，谢绝宾客，曰：「我无私也，我不党也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169038_comment'></div>岂不陋哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169038_comment'></div>谨按谥法：「宠禄光大曰荣」，「不勤成名曰灵」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169038_comment'></div>执中出入将相，以一品就第，可谓「宠禄光大」矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1169038_comment'></div>得位行政，不为不逢，死之日，贤士大夫无述焉，可谓「不勤成名」矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1169038_comment'></div>请合二法，谥曰荣灵。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1169038_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1169039' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169039' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169039?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论陈执中谥荣灵书</a><span class='authorDate'>（嘉祐四年四月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34428, "北宋", "韩维", "poem_title_1169039")'>韩维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169039_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169039'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169039'>臣闻尊卑、亲疏、贤不肖之辨，所以立人伦也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169039_comment'></div>礼者，所以维持人伦，使不斁败之具也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169039_comment'></div>朝廷之位，庙寝之制，车服之数，金石俎豆之容，皆其章也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169039_comment'></div>章不明则尊卑、亲疏、贤不肖之分乱而人伦斁矣，故有天下者不可不先礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169039_comment'></div>窃见国家受命百年，而郊庙之位尚有未正，朝廷之仪尚有未尊，祭祀婚葬车服之等尚多不备，所以然者，患在弃礼而任人情也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169039_comment'></div>夫礼所以撙节人情，使一于正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169039_comment'></div>今任人情而废礼，是以民俗无羞恶之风，士大夫寡廉让之节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169039_comment'></div>制度虽烦，而下不率；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169039_comment'></div>法禁滋密，而奸不胜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1169039_comment'></div>盖有当先而后，宜举而废者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1169039_comment'></div>伏惟皇宋至陛下，比之于周，成、康之时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1169039_comment'></div>方当修起废坠，兴造礼乐，以成一家之制，而典章之失甫有大者，此臣所以不得默也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1169039_comment'></div>臣闻温成之丧，陛下疑所以处中，夜令就陈执中第问之，明日遂发丧皇仪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1169039_comment'></div>由发丧而下，礼之大不可者有四：夫皇仪者，先帝先后之所尝治丧也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1169039_comment'></div>虽宫禁给使之人，知其不当处而处之矣，大不可一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1169039_comment'></div>皇后者，上配宸极，乃天下之母也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1169039_comment'></div>位号至重，岂容僭渎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1169039_comment'></div>中宫在上，而发册殿廷，且以后礼送之，大不可二也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1169039_comment'></div>乐禁之内，大祠用乐者备而不作。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1169039_comment'></div>不祠者，非天地日月则宗庙社稷也，而杀厌其礼，大不可三也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1169039_comment'></div>殿而不庙，不备四时之享者，奉孝惠皇后之礼也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1169039_comment'></div>孝惠皇后者非他，太祖之正配也，犹以为未足而立庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1169039_comment'></div>用乐遂与祖宗等，大不可四也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1169039_comment'></div>别庙四后、章惠皇太后不立忌日久矣，缘此而立之，事已施行，赖陛下圣明，采谏者之言，复止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1169039_comment'></div>不然，此又大不可一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1169039_comment'></div>臣伏思温成皇后虽册位号，其实陛下之后宫也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1169039_comment'></div>今以尊奉后宫，而渎臣主之分，杀天地之祀，僭祖宗之礼，窃料此非陛下本意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1169039_comment'></div>何以言之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1169039_comment'></div>臣伏见陛下谦俭寅畏，谨于事神，笃于奉先，于祠享常礼之外，过自抑损，以极孝恭，不宜有此，盖当时臣下莫为陛下正言者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1169039_comment'></div>陈执中位居师长，无一言之补，夫当国谋事，而至于渎臣主之分，僭祖宗之礼，可谓乖剌矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1169039_comment'></div>生既窃陛下之爵位以厌其欲，若死又得美谥以成其志，是执中终始获幸，而独留非礼之名，使后世有以议陛下也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1169039_comment'></div>臣不胜愤懑，谨因其家请谥，责其大节之失，以「荣灵」加之，盖言其宠禄则厚，而令名不立也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1169039_comment'></div>其义欲使天下知为臣当尽忠，事君当以礼，又使阿谀窃位之臣知生虽茍一时之荣，而死不免万世之戮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1169039_comment'></div>不然，议虚名将朽之骨，臣何独为此区区也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1169039_comment'></div>且谥者，周公所作，万世之公法也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1169039_comment'></div>臣之所言，天下之公议也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1169039_comment'></div>陛下宠待大臣，亦已至矣，而使有司得以万世之公法，天下之公议贬之，亦天下之至公也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1169039_comment'></div>伏惟陛下幸听臣言，以成天下至公之法，岂不大哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1169039_comment'></div>臣备位礼官，凡仪典之违阙，得以讨论，又大臣之薨卒者，得秉笔为议，以善恶谥之，皆臣之职也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1169039_comment'></div>义有所在，不忍缄默。</div><div id='poem_sentence_39_1169039_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1169040' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169040' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169040?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论陈执中直降敕谥恭第一状</a><span class='authorDate'>（嘉祐四年四月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34428, "北宋", "韩维", "poem_title_1169040")'>韩维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169040_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169040'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169040'>臣近与孙抃等议故太师侍中陈执中之谥，论有异同，遂具状申中书门下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169040_comment'></div>臣以谓朝廷且将复下有司，使议执中所以得谥「恭」之状，然后决其是非。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169040_comment'></div>遽闻降敕考功，以「恭」字为定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169040_comment'></div>臣伏思之，不胜皇惑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169040_comment'></div>臣以「荣灵」谥执中者，正谓责其废礼不恭，失为臣之节，而朝廷遂用「恭」法，此臣不得不惑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169040_comment'></div>臣闻孟子曰：「责难于君，谓之恭」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169040_comment'></div>谓以难行之道进于君而勉之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169040_comment'></div>孔子曰：「恭近于礼，远耻辱也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169040_comment'></div>盖礼之意非恭不立，而恭不近礼，适足以招耻辱也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1169040_comment'></div>《书》曰：「官师相规，工执艺事以谏，其或不恭，邦有常刑」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1169040_comment'></div>此言治古之世，自公卿大夫以至百工，各以其职谏，有不如此，谓之不恭也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1169040_comment'></div>执中备位宰相，遭遇明主，若以仁恕临下，赋事行政，惟大臣是咨，惟古训是式，前代人君之所难，陛下皆易之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1169040_comment'></div>此诚人人自竭尽之秋，而执中内怀阿倚，茍援不正之说，僭渎大礼，尚不能成明主之易，可谓责难乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1169040_comment'></div>陛下中宫在上，而妃嫔之没，治丧发册近在殿中，此虽宫省使令之人犹知其不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1169040_comment'></div>执中尚不能及使令之所知，可谓近礼乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1169040_comment'></div>有司上孝惠祠殿之比，不享不乐，罢斥其议，而遂僭祖宗之制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1169040_comment'></div>执中表帅群司，纵不能远复治古，各以职谏，而首自乱礼，此又常刑之所不赦也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1169040_comment'></div>且「恭」之法曰：「不懈于位」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1169040_comment'></div>夫位以宅才，才以治事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1169040_comment'></div>茍事之不治，虽修洁其衣冠，庄严其色辞，终日危坐，无少懈之容，何益哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1169040_comment'></div>执中犯不恭者三，而顾以「恭」为谥，如此则是谥法可废，而官守无用也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1169040_comment'></div>夫设法而至于可废，命官而同于无用，臣愚不识朝廷处此，于义何当？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1169040_comment'></div>伏望陛下亟诏有司格敕未行，复令礼官得尽谥「恭」之说，然后并以臣议下尚书都省，集百官参定。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1169040_comment'></div>臣论有少屈，退伏妄言之诛，诚无所恨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1169040_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1169041' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169041' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169041?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论陈执中直降敕谥恭第二</a><span class='authorDate'>（嘉祐四年四月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34428, "北宋", "韩维", "poem_title_1169041")'>韩维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169041_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169041'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169041'>臣近两上章，论故太师侍中陈执中不当谥「恭」事，至今未蒙朝廷俞允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169041_comment'></div>窃闻敕在考功，有司以不应常法未即奉行，故敢复进其愚说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169041_comment'></div>臣闻圣人治天下，所以得人而用之，其大法有五：士之处也，则教育之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169041_comment'></div>其将进也，则辨论之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169041_comment'></div>其已仕也，则较其功罪而升黜之；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169041_comment'></div>既没也，又作史以纪其善恶，制谥以著其贤不肖。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169041_comment'></div>所以教育奖劝耸惧者如此，故士之为善也固，其远恶也力。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169041_comment'></div>在上者总其才而用之，此天下之所以治也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169041_comment'></div>后世茍简，教育辨论之法既荡然矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1169041_comment'></div>作史制谥，止以备官，而不责其实。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1169041_comment'></div>至于升黜，则非有成可考。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1169041_comment'></div>或举或废，各因其时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1169041_comment'></div>在上者方患才之难得，官之不修，不知所以教育奖劝耸惧之法不立也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1169041_comment'></div>臣请以执中一事明之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1169041_comment'></div>夫执中学问之不讲，义理之不达，而遂至贵显，此「教育」「辨论」已废之验也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1169041_comment'></div>既位宰相，首乱国典，渎尊卑、亲疏之义，而优游寿宠，以一品自终，此「升黜」不行之效也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1169041_comment'></div>今臣区区，欲加公议于已然之后，而同僚不以为得，朝廷不以为善，径黜其论，不少加参考，此又备官而不责其实也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1169041_comment'></div>所未知者，但史官耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1169041_comment'></div>若史官又废其守，则是圣人之法都尽矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1169041_comment'></div>方今风俗颓靡，百职隳惰，谓宜力加振肃，以消因循之弊；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1169041_comment'></div>而乃夺有司之职，使不尽其法；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1169041_comment'></div>退至公之论，使不极其理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1169041_comment'></div>臣恐非朝廷之福也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1169041_comment'></div>伏惟陛下观圣人制法之意，鉴后世茍简之毙，察当今之所宜急，使有司不失其职，公论得有所立，非臣之幸，实天下之幸甚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_23_1169041_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1059&endYear=1059')">1059年9月9日</a>　与欧阳修、刘敞、范镇、江休复、吴奎聚饮梅尧臣家。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1059&endYear=1059')">1059年10月</a>　大拾于太庙,韩维等议礼。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1059&endYear=1059')">1059年5月</a>　上《论温成皇后不当立朝疏》<div id='poem_1169035' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169035' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169035?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论温成皇后不当立庙疏</a><span class='authorDate'>（嘉祐四年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34428, "北宋", "韩维", "poem_title_1169035")'>韩维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169035_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169035'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169035'>臣闻忠臣不为畎亩之远而辍其图报之心，圣主不以刍荛之贱而易其纳善之虑，故下靡不尽之情，上无或遗之策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169035_comment'></div>臣位虽微贱，然以讨论载籍、参议典礼为职。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169035_comment'></div>窃不自薄，有爱君之言，惟陛下少加听览。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169035_comment'></div>臣伏见国家为温成皇后立庙，备三献官，设五时之祭，金石牢具一依宗庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169035_comment'></div>臣上求《礼经》，下循本朝故事，皆所未有。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169035_comment'></div>不知当时谁为陛下画此谋者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169035_comment'></div>臣闻孝惠皇后，太祖皇帝之正配也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169035_comment'></div>其没也，即陵构殿；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169035_comment'></div>岁时所祀，不过常馔而已；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1169035_comment'></div>其后方得列于皇后别庙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1169035_comment'></div>元德皇后，真宗皇帝之母也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1169035_comment'></div>其没也，别庙而祭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1169035_comment'></div>自尔群臣请升祔相继，先帝慎重其事，不敢即从，至于十年而后许之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1169035_comment'></div>今陛下一旦奉嫔御之主庙，而享之与祖宗等，稽于先王之礼则不合，求之本朝之事则非故，搢绅之士无所诵说，下民观之不知所化，甚非太祖、真宗慎重典礼之深旨也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1169035_comment'></div>伏惟陛下即位以来，凡所兴造，必问于遗训而咨于故实，稀阔盛事，靡不毕讲。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1169035_comment'></div>今又将以孟冬吉时亲祼宗庙，修大祫之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1169035_comment'></div>盖祫者，序昭穆、正尊卑之祭也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1169035_comment'></div>所宜罢斥不端，昭示大顺，以成祀典之美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1169035_comment'></div>而陛下以奉祖宗之礼而臣妾亦得享之，非所以致隆极、广孝恭也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1169035_comment'></div>臣愚以为宜因此时发德音，诏有司，使议温成皇后之庙，有不如礼者一皆裁去，以明陛下不私后宫、专奉祖宗之意，使圣朝典制幽昧复光，宗庙神灵欢欣顾享，此盛德之举也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1169035_comment'></div>陛下不可不加圣意焉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1169035_comment'></div>昔汉文帝幸上林，袁盎引却慎夫人之坐，以明妾主之义，前史书之，烂然不忘。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1169035_comment'></div>今崇建庙祀，甚于上林之坐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1169035_comment'></div>僭拟祖宗，非特妾主之别。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1169035_comment'></div>陛下圣德过于汉文，毋使愚臣不得申袁盎之志。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1169035_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_25_1169035'>〔贴黄一〕陛下若以温成皇后久在左右，不忘轸悼，则岁时遣宫嫔内侍厚加祭奠，亦足致其恩意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1169035_comment'></div>何必僭用礼典，取讥后代？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1169035_comment'></div>此于温成皇后非有所益，而于圣德为损不细。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1169035_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_28_1169035'>〔贴黄二〕陛下即位以来，动循礼典，未尝有此过举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1169035_comment'></div>臣愿陛下特奋神断，使有司得从改正，以全盛德之美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1169035_comment'></div>臣父子受国厚恩，实欲以此少申补报，幸不以臣位下而弃其言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1169035_comment'></div>《南阳集》卷二二。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_31_1169035'></div><div id='poem_sentence_31_1169035_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1063&endYear=1063')">1063年4月</a>　拟《请皇太后权同听政诏》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1063&endYear=1063')">1063年9月</a>　为太常丞,充记室参军。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1063&endYear=1063')">1063年12月</a>　兼充检讨官。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1064&endYear=1064')">1064年6月</a>　为直集贤院、诸王府记室参军。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1064&endYear=1064')">1064年12月</a>　修起居注。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1064&endYear=1064')">1064年</a>　拟《文思副使内侍押班王昭明可右骇骥副使制》<div id='poem_1168894' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1168894' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1168894?labeling=true' target='_blank'>文思副使内侍押班王昭明可右骐骥副使制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1064年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34428, "北宋", "韩维", "poem_title_1168894")'>韩维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1168894_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1168894'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1168894'>敕某：夫入侍轩墀，帅属以祗事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1168894_comment'></div>出守疆埸，提兵以御侮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1168894_comment'></div>非吾信谨之臣，不以任也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1168894_comment'></div>尔夙尚忠固，兼资才武，在职不懈，有劳当迁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1168894_comment'></div>稍升使领之华，尚仍边守之旧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1168894_comment'></div>益茂乃绩，毋忝朕恩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1168894_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1168894_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年8月</a>　宋敏求、韩维同修《仁宗实录》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年9月</a>　拟《给事中权御史中压贾黯可依前官充翰林侍读学士知陈州制》<div id='poem_1168856' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1168856' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1168856?labeling=true' target='_blank'>给事中权御史中丞贾黯可依前官充翰林侍读学士知陈州制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1065年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34428, "北宋", "韩维", "poem_title_1168856")'>韩维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1168856_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1168856'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1168856'>敕：朝之近臣，朕所优礼，入则备台阁之领，出则膺翰垣之任，委属之重，厥惟均哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1168856_comment'></div>具官某，气质方厚，学术雅正，操尚不移于流俗，论议有益于当世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1168856_comment'></div>朕方付以宪司之纲纪、史氏之笔削，而引疾来上，请藩自便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1168856_comment'></div>言念诚至，可无俞允。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1168856_comment'></div>俾兼进读之职，往分卧治之寄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1168856_comment'></div>善辅尔体，以及吾民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1168856_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1168856_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年10月</a>　拟《给事中充天章阁待制彭思永可依前权御史中压充理检使制》<div id='poem_1168892' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1168892' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1168892?labeling=true' target='_blank'>给事中充天章阁待制彭思永可依前权御史中丞充理检使制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1065年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34428, "北宋", "韩维", "poem_title_1168892")'>韩维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1168892_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1168892'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1168892'>敕：御史大夫官废久矣，惟中丞实长其府事，非操行沈雅可仪于人，论议刚明不阿乎世者，恶能胜其任哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1168892_comment'></div>具官某，质厚而有守，和乐而不流，器能足以任重，风迹可以起顽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1168892_comment'></div>往持御史之笔，见称简直；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1168892_comment'></div>荐分使者之节，多所效正。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1168892_comment'></div>夫入拜琐闼，于古为重；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1168892_comment'></div>进长宪府，如前之审。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1168892_comment'></div>历选于众，无以易汝。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1168892_comment'></div>朕欲纪纲之振修、号令之明慎，而疾夫流俗之人，袭茍简以败官，怀阿倚以事上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1168892_comment'></div>尔其为朕督察，以时绳举，尚俾予治，毋愧于前人之休。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1168892_comment'></div>往其懋哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1168892_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1168892_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年7月</a>　上《乞询问讲读臣寮状》<div id='poem_1169045' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169045' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169045?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞询问讲读臣寮状</a><span class='authorDate'>（治平二年七月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34428, "北宋", "韩维", "poem_title_1169045")'>韩维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169045_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169045'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169045'>臣幸得以史官侍左右记言动，窃见每开迩英阁召近臣讲读经史，陛下未尝一发德音，有所询问。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169045_comment'></div>遂使执经者不得极其说，秉笔者无所载其美，已事而退，莫不俛默，有不自得之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169045_comment'></div>臣窃惑之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169045_comment'></div>臣闻傅说有言：「王人求多闻，时惟建事」，「事不师古，以克永世，匪说攸闻」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169045_comment'></div>盖治天下者必先于建事，欲建事者莫重于师古，欲师古者莫急于求多闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169045_comment'></div>然则今之所谓讲筵者，陛下之所以求多闻也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169045_comment'></div>尧舜圣帝必先稽古，三代令主皆有师傅之官，坐论道义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169045_comment'></div>尔后德薄不能如古，然至于欲治之主，亦莫不以此为急。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169045_comment'></div>汉高祖初得天下，感陆贾之言，知不可以马上治之，每奏《新语》，篇篇称善，光武数引公卿郎将讲论经理，夜分乃寐；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1169045_comment'></div>唐太宗命学士杜如晦等十八人更直阁下，降以温颜，与之讨论经义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1169045_comment'></div>此数君者，岂乐勤苦而徇虚名哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1169045_comment'></div>诚以治天下之要莫不出此，故功业隆于当时，声名流于后世，非其幸也，其道有以致之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1169045_comment'></div>朝廷自宰相以及群司，率以职事进退，所言皆目前常务，而又迫景晷，不得详尽其理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1169045_comment'></div>迩英阁者，陛下燕閒之所也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1169045_comment'></div>侍于侧者，皆献纳论思之臣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1169045_comment'></div>陈于前者，非圣人之经则历代之史也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1169045_comment'></div>御閒燕则可以留漏刻之永，对侍臣则可以极咨访之博，论经史则可以穷仁义之道、祸败之原。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1169045_comment'></div>起而行之，则上可以为尧舜三代之君，下犹不失为汉高、光武、唐太宗也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1169045_comment'></div>然非从容降接则无以尽臣下之情，非往复研究则无以见圣人之奥，非力而行之则不足以追前古之治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1169045_comment'></div>陛下于此三者似未尽之，此臣所以不得不惑也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1169045_comment'></div>至于群臣，亦皆惑之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1169045_comment'></div>议者以为陛下向在亮阴，惟于咨决政事有不得已而言耳，其馀可得而略也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1169045_comment'></div>今礼制终毕，臣下倾耳以听玉音。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1169045_comment'></div>语曰：「时然后言」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1169045_comment'></div>陛下之言，此其时也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1169045_comment'></div>臣虽不敏，请秉笔以俟。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1169045_comment'></div>干冒天威，臣无任惶惧战越恳激之至<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1169045_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_27_1169045'>有：原无，据《国朝诸臣奏议》补。</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1169045_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1169045'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_26_1169045_0'>⑴ 《南阳集》卷二三。又见《东都事略》卷五八，《国朝诸臣奏议》卷五○，《历代名臣奏议》卷六，《宋元通鉴》卷二九，《古文渊鉴》卷五四。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1169045_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1065&endYear=1065')">1065年</a>　上《乞亲谕使人救济饥民状》<div id='poem_1169046' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169046' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169046?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞亲谕使人救济饥民状</a><span class='authorDate'>（治平二年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34428, "北宋", "韩维", "poem_title_1169046")'>韩维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169046_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169046'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169046'>臣窃闻去年开封府界并、陈、蔡、许、颍等州岁各不熟，入春以来，民困尤甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169046_comment'></div>朝廷虽发仓廪，转米谷以加赈赡，而死者不可胜数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169046_comment'></div>其甚者至于遗弃幼稚，号哭道路，骨肉之间，自相啖食，僵尸暴骸，所在狼籍，闻之可为伤痛。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169046_comment'></div>臣日夜思念，盖赈救之道有所未尽，以及于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169046_comment'></div>州县米谷之不积，一也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169046_comment'></div>官吏无恤民之心，二也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169046_comment'></div>饲养失处置之宜，三也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169046_comment'></div>朝廷虽发仓廪，而陛下未尝亲谕恻怛之意，遣使临视，四也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169046_comment'></div>群议籍籍，窃怪陛下勤政爱民，日昃不倦，至于细务，莫不曲加处分，而于此事，未闻德音有所矜恤，意者陛下未知其详与？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1169046_comment'></div>臣闻群议且久，每欲上闻，以越职为惧而止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1169046_comment'></div>今前去二麦尚有数月，而死者日广，臣诚不忍陛下赤子遭逢仁圣之君，不得蒙被其泽，而无告以死，臣虽越职得罪，犹不敢避也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1169046_comment'></div>伏望圣慈特诏执政择爱民干事之吏十数辈，召见便坐，喻以忧劳悯伤之意，令分使州县，察视流民，先具见存及死亡之数与守令救济之状以闻，然后与转运、提刑、知州、通判等同共疾速商量如何处置救养，可以全活民命；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1169046_comment'></div>比至麦熟，合用米粮几何，如何营救，不至乏绝；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1169046_comment'></div>不幸死者，所在官为掩瘗，毋得暴露。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1169046_comment'></div>凡此诸事，皆许入马铺驰奏，陛下与二府大臣朝夕图议，茍国家之力可及之者，无不为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1169046_comment'></div>如此则庶几斯民渐有生路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1169046_comment'></div>不然，三四十万之众，至四五月之间，皆填沟壑矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1169046_comment'></div>臣闻天之所以祐命人君者，将以牧民也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1169046_comment'></div>君之所以享尊极者，以有民为之下也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1169046_comment'></div>民之所以欣戴其上者，以能保安己也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1169046_comment'></div>陛下即位之初，宜有以固结天下之心，而副天之所以祐命者，无急于此也，臣愿陛下力行之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1169046_comment'></div>干冒天威，臣无任涕泗激切之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_21_1169046_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1066&endYear=1066')">1066年1月</a>　上《论范镇请郡劄子》<div id='poem_1169060' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169060' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169060?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论范镇请郡劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（治平三年正月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34428, "北宋", "韩维", "poem_title_1169060")'>韩维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169060_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169060'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169060'>臣窃闻翰林学士范镇上章求补郡，外议藉藉，皆以为陛下以镇作宰相批答不称旨，谕令解去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169060_comment'></div>不知此事虚实果如此者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169060_comment'></div>臣窃为陛下不取。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169060_comment'></div>镇诚有罪，自可明正典刑；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169060_comment'></div>若其所失止在文字之间，茍非甚悖义理，犹当涵容，以全待近臣之体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169060_comment'></div>陛下前黜钱公辅，中外莫不以为太重，至或相传，谓公辅别有过慝，主上不欲暴扬，故行遣至此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169060_comment'></div>陛下连退二近臣，而众人皆不晓然知其所谓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169060_comment'></div>臣恐自此臣下各怀疑惧，莫敢为陛下尽心者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169060_comment'></div>镇今既从其自请，例须换职领郡，于镇何损？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1169060_comment'></div>但可惜者，陛下不明朝廷赏罚耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1169060_comment'></div>臣近对延和，尝论人君好恶，当明见赏罚，以示天下，使人知所从违，则风俗可移。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1169060_comment'></div>又以为虽圣贤思虑不能全无过差，假如陛下误有处分，改之则足章纳善从谏之美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1169060_comment'></div>此语甚近，陛下亦应记省。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1169060_comment'></div>臣骤蒙拔擢，不敢俯默，自同众人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1169060_comment'></div>伏望圣慈，察臣向者所言，更于此事精加思虑，及其未有成命，速赐回革，所冀不至上累圣德。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1169060_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1066&endYear=1066')">1066年1月</a>　兼领通进银台司门下封驳事,上《论敕不由银台司劄》<div id='poem_1169052' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169052' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169052?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论敕不由银台司劄</a><span class='authorDate'>（治平三年正月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34428, "北宋", "韩维", "poem_title_1169052")'>韩维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169052_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169052'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169052'>臣近以黜吕诲等敕，不由门下封驳司，尝面具论奏及两上章乞正官法，并未蒙圣恩施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169052_comment'></div>臣伏以纪纲法度，圣王所以维持邦国，使不危而安者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169052_comment'></div>其所措意皆关盛衰，固不为一日设也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169052_comment'></div>譬之犹舟之有维楫，马之有衔辔。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169052_comment'></div>今有人于此，将假二物以出万里之涂，而自毁其维楫，绝其衔辔，则人人知其有奔偾沈溺之忧矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169052_comment'></div>臣近对崇政殿，亦尝以此理上陈，陛下初不省察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169052_comment'></div>又以失职求赐罢斥，而圣慈再三敦谕，不令投进文字。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169052_comment'></div>臣僶俛而退，犹望陛下悟前之失，特诏有司修明旧法，以防将来之患。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169052_comment'></div>而章上辄不出，使臣不得少申职业，坐守空名，以蒙贪禄旷官之谤，进退实亦难处。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1169052_comment'></div>伏望圣慈，以臣此状并前两奏降付中书门下商量施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1169052_comment'></div>臣不敢枉道以阿人主之意，爱身以坏祖宗之法，惟陛下裁处。</div><div id='poem_sentence_10_1169052_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1066&endYear=1066')">1066年2月</a>　上书。作品：《乞还吕诲等职事劄子》《论吕诲等勅不由封驳司劄》《再论吕诲等勅不由封驳司劄子》《论救不由银台司待罪劄子》《缴纳举台官勅劄子》《缴纳举台官勅劄子》<div id='poem_1169048' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169048' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169048?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞还吕诲等职事劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（治平三年正月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34428, "北宋", "韩维", "poem_title_1169048")'>韩维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169048_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169048'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169048'>臣窃闻御史知杂吕诲等，以论濮安懿王事得罪，并行谴逐，群议喧然，皆以为诲等能审义守职，国之忠臣，而窃叹朝廷典刑遂至于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169048_comment'></div>臣伏念陛下自入继大统，士大夫莫不首论为人后之大义，以为陛下素好经术，必能循用礼典，以副先帝顾托之意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169048_comment'></div>自两制之议上闻，臣下更白交谏，务欲上广聪明，以正此事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169048_comment'></div>而今者遂至斥逐宪官，以失天下之望，诚可痛也！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169048_comment'></div>台官之言，臣虽不尽闻，料其用心，不过欲陛下尽如先王之法而止耳。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169048_comment'></div>即如此者，乃是爱君之至，安所得罪而逐之也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169048_comment'></div>近年以来，风俗颓敝，士大夫类皆贪固宠利，护惜人情，姑息茍且，为自容之计，莫肯为国家悉心营职者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169048_comment'></div>陛下厚赏以劝之，严罚以督之，犹恐此风不变，而复内牵邪说，贬斥正人，数以微过放远善士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169048_comment'></div>臣恐自此奸倖得志，忠良结舌，陛下耳目日益壅蔽，缓急朝廷有事，上无由知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1169048_comment'></div>此时虽欲悔恨，亦无及矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1169048_comment'></div>方今法度隳废，百职不治，国用匮乏，民力凋困；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1169048_comment'></div>外无良将，士卒骄惰，彊敌窥间而有轻中国之心；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1169048_comment'></div>而天灾数见，地变复作，疾疫流行，饥馑荐至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1169048_comment'></div>由此观之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1169048_comment'></div>臣恐陛下之忧不在濮王名号未崇，台官不畏威听命也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1169048_comment'></div>伏望圣慈，思社稷安危之计，以人情去就为虑，亟追昨日诏书，还诲等职事，以救前失，以安群情。</div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_1169048'></div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1169048_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1169050' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169050' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169050?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论吕诲等敕不由封驳司劄</a><span class='authorDate'>（治平三年正月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34428, "北宋", "韩维", "poem_title_1169050")'>韩维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169050_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169050'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169050'>臣昨日闻御史知杂吕诲等以言事被斥，至今不见敕，至封驳司访问，乃是中书直封送本家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169050_comment'></div>臣窃以封驳司，给事中之任也，凡制敕必由此而下，有所不便，得以封还论奏，古今之通制也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169050_comment'></div>今罢斥御史，事关政体，而遂不使有司预闻，纪纲之失，无甚于此。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169050_comment'></div>臣伏思王者建立官局，张设法度，择人守之，所以防检缪失，共成治道，而朝廷自坏其法，不知为此将以何利也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169050_comment'></div>伏望圣慈，指挥中书追还诲等敕命，令由本司使臣得申论议，以正陛下之官法<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169050_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_1169050'>司：原脱，据明钞本、《国朝诸臣奏议》补。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1169050_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1169050'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_4_1169050_0'>⑴ 《南阳集》卷二三。又见《国朝诸臣奏议》卷五六，《历代名臣奏议》卷一六○。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1169050_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_1169051' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169051' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169051?labeling=true' target='_blank'>再论吕诲等敕不由封驳司劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（治平三年正月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34428, "北宋", "韩维", "poem_title_1169051")'>韩维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169051_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169051'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169051'>臣近以御史知杂吕诲等降斥敕命，不由门下封驳司，直送本家，尝具论奏乞追还，以正官法。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169051_comment'></div>至今累日，未见施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169051_comment'></div>臣伏思古者并建庶官，各有法式，所以共成治道，远防祸败，虽王者不得而私也，况大臣乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169051_comment'></div>淳化中，命枢密直学士向敏中、张咏检点看读发放敕命，其实封驳文，并仰中书逐房候印押下送向敏中等看读检点了却，实封发放。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169051_comment'></div>祖宗所以慎重号令，防检谬失如此其至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169051_comment'></div>今朝廷一旦骋私意以坏圣王之法，快目前而忘后世之虑，独何谓也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169051_comment'></div>方今官失其法，人怠其职，百事隳废，日就衰靡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169051_comment'></div>臣愚窃谓宜有以力振颓敝，而陛下君臣方共为此事，臣窃为国家忧之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169051_comment'></div>伏望圣慈，以臣此奏并前所上章早降付中书施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1169051_comment'></div>臣庸懦不能为陛下守官，伏待谴黜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1169051_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_1169051'>〔贴黄〕臣昨日崇政殿面陈失职，欲望夺臣知制诰，乞一小郡差遣，蒙陛下再三宣谕，不令陈请。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1169051_comment'></div>虽上体圣意，不敢即投文字，然臣为陛下守官，而不能修整法度，实恐终亦难处。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1169051_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1169055' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169055' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169055?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论敕不由银台司待罪劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（治平三年二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34428, "北宋", "韩维", "poem_title_1169055")'>韩维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169055_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169055'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169055'>臣近以降黜吕诲等敕命不由银台司，累具论奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169055_comment'></div>今又闻罢傅尧俞等敕，亦是直送本家。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169055_comment'></div>臣窃以法制者，天下之公器，非天子所得私而有，而臣下所敢辄废也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169055_comment'></div>故法有不便事则易之，未有设而不行者；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169055_comment'></div>人有不称职则去之，未有存而不用者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169055_comment'></div>陛下才毕亮阴，即降诏戒厉臣下，曰：「内外因循惰职者众，未闻推利及民，尽心忧国者」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169055_comment'></div>其末又训以「易虑孳孳，各循厥职」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169055_comment'></div>诏下以来，未及一年，不闻群司有所进益，而公卿大臣方自坏法度，违失诏文。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169055_comment'></div>臣虽区区，为陛下爱惜此事，章三四上，不蒙省察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1169055_comment'></div>京都之内，禁门之中，尚且如此，而欲以风劝天下，推利及民，岂可得哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1169055_comment'></div>孟子有言曰：「有官守者，不得其职则去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1169055_comment'></div>有言责者，不得其言则去」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1169055_comment'></div>今有言责者，既不得而去矣，不得其职者，尚且胡颜以苟处乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1169055_comment'></div>况臣两还诏旨，今又不能仰遵圣谕，为官守法，罪戾仍重，岂宜久玷侍从，尚窃封驳之名？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1169055_comment'></div>伏望圣慈特赐黜罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1169055_comment'></div>所有银台司等职事，臣更不敢签书，见居家待罪。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1169055_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_1169053' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169053' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169053?labeling=true' target='_blank'>缴纳举台官敕劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（治平三年二月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34428, "北宋", "韩维", "poem_title_1169053")'>韩维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169053_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169053'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169053'>臣昨日閤门送到敕一道，令臣举官二人充御史。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169053_comment'></div>臣伏以知人之道，古今至难，故圣王取士之法必有所试，见其迹效可用，然后升进，乃不失人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169053_comment'></div>臣伏见吕诲等刚果强劲，守义不回，至于犯死亡之诛，不顾忌讳，以尽论议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169053_comment'></div>求之古今，如此至少。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169053_comment'></div>臣又闻陛下向者自出范纯仁、吕大防二人之姓名，令除御史，众见纯仁等能竭节言事，皆谓陛下明哲，选任得人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169053_comment'></div>纯仁等不负陛下所知，得事君报国之道，今一旦斥逐，士大夫莫不窃叹痛惜。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169053_comment'></div>陛下毁已成之美，受可耻之名，失当世之属望，而贻后代之讥议。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169053_comment'></div>今奉敕旨，令别举御史，臣伏自惟，度臣之驽下，何敢少望清光？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169053_comment'></div>虽欲慎举，岂如圣主之自择？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1169053_comment'></div>又人未试用，诚亦难知。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1169053_comment'></div>如诲等则有已试之效矣，陛下必欲为官求人，采群言以兴至治，则臣愿复二人者以佐陛下招贤纳谏之美。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1169053_comment'></div>其举台官敕，臣已具公文缴还閤门，未敢祇受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1169053_comment'></div>干冒天威，臣无任惶惧陨越激切之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1169053_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1066&endYear=1066')">1066年3月</a>　上《乞不汎于诸家为颖王择妃状》<div id='poem_1169059' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169059' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169059?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞不汎于诸家为颖王择妃状</a><span class='authorDate'>（治平三年三月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34428, "北宋", "韩维", "poem_title_1169059")'>韩维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169059_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169059'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169059'>臣累日以来，传闻禁中汎至诸臣之家，为颖王择妃，审如此者，臣窃以为非便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169059_comment'></div>臣闻夫妇者，居室之大伦，将以正家则，承宗事，以继万世之嗣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169059_comment'></div>故礼之用，惟昏姻为兢兢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169059_comment'></div>兢兢者，慎之至也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169059_comment'></div>《坊记》曰：「诸侯不下<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_4_1169059", 1169059, "Clauses/15/Comments/1")'>渔色</span>，故君子远色以为民纪」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169059_comment'></div>此言诸侯不得自于其国网取容色，若捕渔然，所以推远女色，为民之纪法也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169059_comment'></div>伏以皇子颍王孝友聪明，动履法度，方向经义，以观成德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169059_comment'></div>今卜族授室，其系尤重，臣愚以为宜历选勋望之家，慎择淑哲之媛，考古纳采问名之义，以礼成之，不宜茍取华色而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169059_comment'></div>近世简弃礼教，不以为务。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1169059_comment'></div>婚娶之法，自朝廷以及民庶，荡然无制。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1169059_comment'></div>故风俗颓靡，犯礼者众。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1169059_comment'></div>贤士大夫未尝不发愤太息，窃幸国家有以振之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1169059_comment'></div>今陛下始初清明，为元子求妇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1169059_comment'></div>而事出茍简，殆非所以矫世厉俗，反之雅正，且无以示颖王，使知室家之道在德而不在色也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1169059_comment'></div>传称「尤物足以移人」，《诗》咏淑女「端为风始」，此诚智士仁人见微知终，远览祸福之原，为后世戒也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1169059_comment'></div>陛下不可不加圣意焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1169059_comment'></div>臣获侍宸陛，且官王府，茍益万一，不敢不言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1169059_comment'></div>干冒天威，臣无任惶惧激切之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1169059_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1066&endYear=1066')">1066年3月</a>　拟《左司郎中充天章阁待制兼侍读李受可左谏议大夫依前侍制兼侍读徐如故制》<div id='poem_1168850' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1168850' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1168850?labeling=true' target='_blank'>左司郎中充天章阁待制兼侍读李受可左谏议大夫依前待制兼侍读馀如故制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1066年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34428, "北宋", "韩维", "poem_title_1168850")'>韩维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1168850_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1168850'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1168850'>敕：夫入直延阁，以备顾问，出侍露门，以参进读，皆所以敷道古训，启迪朕志，其于事效固不待考而后著也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1168850_comment'></div>具官某，服道淳固，秉心易直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1168850_comment'></div>被先帝之慎选，首充调护；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1168850_comment'></div>逮冲人之纂服，弥见忠益。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1168850_comment'></div>畴其履阅之茂，立于谏诤之列。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1168850_comment'></div>嘉谋至言，朕所望于耆德也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1168850_comment'></div>君其勉之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1168850_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1168850_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1067&endYear=1067')">1067年1月</a>　权同知贡举。作品：《论遗赐劄子》<div id='poem_1169063' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169063' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169063?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论遗赐劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（治平四年正月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34428, "北宋", "韩维", "poem_title_1169063")'>韩维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169063_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169063'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169063'>臣窃闻故事，大行皇帝当有遗留物分赐臣下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169063_comment'></div>臣伏思承平日久，用度无节，以致公私匮乏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169063_comment'></div>又国家不幸，四年之内，两遭大故，营造山陵及支士卒优赏，所费不可胜计。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169063_comment'></div>今之府库，比于仁宗晚年，又益朘削，若用嘉祐之例，厚行赐赉，臣恐为损不小。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169063_comment'></div>陛下若以为奉承先帝之志，加惠群臣，不可罢止，则望阅诸府库，取服用玩好之物以充用，才足将意便可，不须过为丰侈。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169063_comment'></div>所有金帛诸物可以赡兵恤民者，愿赐爱惜，以救当世之积毙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169063_comment'></div>取进止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169063_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_1169063'>〔贴黄〕陛下于此时即位，正当躬行勤俭，帅先天下，以彊国阜民为意者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169063_comment'></div>若以臣言为然，则请从此一事为始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1169063_comment'></div>况遗留之赐，自台谏官以上方始有之，此等皆朝廷旧臣，义当体国，虽至薄约，万无不足之理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1169063_comment'></div>若泛及庶僚，恐反为陛下累者，臣实不敢妄言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1169063_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1169063_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1067&endYear=1067')">1067年2月</a>　除龙图阁直学士。作品：《初御殿进劄子》<div id='poem_1169065' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169065' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169065?labeling=true' target='_blank'>初御殿进劄子</a><span class='authorDate'>（治平四年二月乙酉）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34428, "北宋", "韩维", "poem_title_1169065")'>韩维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169065_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169065'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169065'>臣窃闻陛下以来，日御便殿听政，臣愚虑所及，辄有三事，以为慎终正本之助，幸陛下省察。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169065_comment'></div>一者陛下新罹大忧，方当以思亲摧慕为意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169065_comment'></div>从权听政，盖是不得已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169065_comment'></div>意者惟大事急务，特赐裁决，其馀可阔略。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169065_comment'></div>故事，始见群臣及降坐入宫，皆举音呜咽，此高宗亮阴不言之意也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169065_comment'></div>二者执政皆两朝顾命大臣，人君所当与共图天下之务者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169065_comment'></div>陛下即位之初，尤宜推诚加礼，每事咨访，以尽其心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169065_comment'></div>至于博谋群臣，究极理道，虽是美德，止可密裨圣虑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169065_comment'></div>及至决议论，发号令，必须经由二府施行，乃合政体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1169065_comment'></div>周公戒伯禽曰：「不使大臣怨乎不以」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1169065_comment'></div>盖谓此也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1169065_comment'></div>三者百执事各有职分，惟当责任，使人尽其能。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1169065_comment'></div>若王者代有司行事，最为失体。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1169065_comment'></div>孔子曰「先有司」是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1169065_comment'></div>三体既正矣，若夫恭己倡率，随事裁处，则一系圣断也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1169065_comment'></div>天下大事不可猝为，人君施设自有先后，惟陛下加意慎重，以副四海观望。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1169065_comment'></div>臣不胜苦切涕泗之至。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1169065_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_17_1169065_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1067&endYear=1067')">1067年3月</a>　拟《工部郎中知制诰王安石可旧官服阕制》<div id='poem_1168877' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1168877' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1168877?labeling=true' target='_blank'>工部郎中知制诰王安石可旧官服阕制</a><span class='authorDate'>（1067年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34428, "北宋", "韩维", "poem_title_1168877")'>韩维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1168877_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1168877'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1168877'>敕：三年之丧，禄之于家，而不敢烦以事，此朝廷所以待近臣而申孝子之情也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1168877_comment'></div>若夫既除而从政，则下之所当勉也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1168877_comment'></div>具官某，学通经术，行应法义，衔哀服礼，内外竭尽，可谓邦之俊良，民之表仪者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1168877_comment'></div>朕临政愿治久矣，想闻生之奇论，以佐不逮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1168877_comment'></div>其悉朕意，亟复于位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1168877_comment'></div>可。</div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1168877_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1067&endYear=1067')">1067年3月</a>　上《议召王安石割子》作品：《议召王安石劄子》<div id='poem_1169066' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169066' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169066?labeling=true' target='_blank'>议召王安石劄子<span class='inlineComment2'>（治平四年闰三月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1067年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34428, "北宋", "韩维", "poem_title_1169066")'>韩维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169066_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169066'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169066'>臣今日传闻除王安石知江宁府，然未知事之信否。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169066_comment'></div>若诚然者，臣窃以为非所以致安石也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169066_comment'></div>何则？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169066_comment'></div>安石守正知道，不为利动，其于出处之际，谅已素定于心，必不妄发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169066_comment'></div>今安石久病不朝，若一旦除大郡，即起视事，则是安石偃蹇君命，苟禄自便，臣固知安石之不肯为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169066_comment'></div>又其精神困弊，今除一大郡，而反不能奉朝请，从容侍从之间，岂复人情？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169066_comment'></div>臣又知安石之不肯为也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169066_comment'></div>所可致者，其惟一事，即陛下向所宣谕，臣向所开陈者是也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169066_comment'></div>夫人君始初践阼，慨然想见贤哲，与图天下之事，孰不愿效其忠，伸其道哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1169066_comment'></div>使安石甚庸碌者则已，若不至此，必幡然而来矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1169066_comment'></div>臣窃恐议者以为安石可以渐致，而不可以猝召，若如此，是诱之也，是不知安石者之言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1169066_comment'></div>惟贤者可以义动而不可以计取，陛下稽古讲道，必于此理灿然无惑，惟在断而行之，毋以前议为疑，则天下幸甚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1169066_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1067&endYear=1067')">1067年4月</a>　上《论宰相与中丞得失状》<div id='poem_1169068' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169068' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169068?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论宰相与中丞得失状</a><span class='authorDate'>（治平四年四月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34428, "北宋", "韩维", "poem_title_1169068")'>韩维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169068_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169068'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169068'>右臣窃闻御史中丞王陶等言宰相跋扈及除用不当。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169068_comment'></div>昨日传闻罢陶中丞，还旧职，既而又闻除翰林学士，今早又闻参知政事吴奎夺职待罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169068_comment'></div>台谏官请对论事，相继不绝，中外汹汹，忧疑震骇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169068_comment'></div>而风霾日兴，旱暵滋甚，滥炎数发，寒燠不常，天人之情，可谓至不和矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169068_comment'></div>臣伏思天下所以君君臣臣父父子子而莫敢乱者，以义理存也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169068_comment'></div>义理者非他，是是而非非也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169068_comment'></div>人君者，明义理，别是非，以治天下者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169068_comment'></div>宰相者，天下所信任；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169068_comment'></div>御史中丞，天子所咨决。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1169068_comment'></div>今御史中丞言宰相跋扈，即有是事，则是王法之所诛也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1169068_comment'></div>陛下若以御史中丞言为信，则宰相安得不罪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1169068_comment'></div>若其不然，则是御史中丞构造邪说，离间陛下君臣，其罪岂止罢去而已！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1169068_comment'></div>若又除翰林学士，是迁之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1169068_comment'></div>陛下既不能明辨大臣，示信任不疑之意，以尽其心，又使言者无名罢去，疑惑远方，谓陛下不能纳谏，频黜宪官。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1169068_comment'></div>臣虽忝备近侍，尚不知陛下之罢王陶所言为是邪，为非邪？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1169068_comment'></div>若以为是，则陶乃称职，不可轻罢；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1169068_comment'></div>若其非也，岂当更迁其官？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1169068_comment'></div>此臣不得不言也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1169068_comment'></div>臣且惑之，欲令四方不疑，难矣！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1169068_comment'></div>两朝顾命大臣，陛下不能主张辨明，使负恶名，有不自安之意，则其下者岂肯为陛下尽心？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1169068_comment'></div>中丞在天子左右，言之是非，陛下不能裁察，则远者岂肯为陛下尽言？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1169068_comment'></div>陛下即位之初，将收天下之心，尽众庶之言，别白邪正，协和上下，以举大治，而今者是非杂糅，贤不肖淆乱，群情暌乖，日益偷惰。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1169068_comment'></div>人事尚且如此，欲望天道之顺序，岂不甚难哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1169068_comment'></div>臣愿陛下廷对群臣，面问宰相跋扈之状，及御史中丞所言如何，使是非一判，邪正两辨，然后断自宸虑，大行显黜，以开天下之耳目。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1169068_comment'></div>此事若不明辨，臣恐朝廷刑政自此衰敝，不复振矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1169068_comment'></div>若臣所言幸蒙施用，则事辨之后，乞罢臣职任，授一小州，或留台閒官，以明臣一心为陛下忠计，非有爱憎向背于其间也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1169068_comment'></div>臣窃闻众人惮陶，及以朋附大臣为嫌，莫肯正言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1169068_comment'></div>臣幸得以宫府旧僚蒙被知遇，不敢爱身以废公议，惟陛下特留圣意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1169068_comment'></div>干冒宸严，臣无任战汗陨越忠愤之至，谨具状奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_28_1169068_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1067&endYear=1067')">1067年4月</a>　上《论吴奎罢参政奏》<div id='poem_1169110' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169110' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169110?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论吴奎罢参政奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（治平四年四月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34428, "北宋", "韩维", "poem_title_1169110")'>韩维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169110_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169110'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169110'>奎素有学问，敦笃持重，可任以事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169110_comment'></div>擢参大政，众谓得人。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169110_comment'></div>今才数月，止因论事之际，少失婉顺，便加斥逐，进退大臣，不当如是。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1169110_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1169110'><span class='label'>按：</span>《三朝名臣言行录》卷一○之二，四部丛刊本。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1169110_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1067&endYear=1067')">1067年4月</a>　上《论吴奎迁官奏》<div id='poem_1169111' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169111' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169111?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论吴奎迁官奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（治平四年四月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34428, "北宋", "韩维", "poem_title_1169111")'>韩维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169111_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169111'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169111'>执政罢免，则为降黜；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169111_comment'></div>今复迁官，则为褒进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169111_comment'></div>二者理难并行，此与王陶罢中丞而加学士何以异？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169111_comment'></div>赏罚所以为天下之耳目，岂可不慎。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169111_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1169111_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1169111'><span class='label'>按：</span>《三朝名臣言行录》卷一○之二，四部丛刊本。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1169111_comment'></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='397f8919fea34c05871592275c86bc56_label'><a href='javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1069&endYear=1071')">1069-1071年</a>，53-55岁</div><div id='397f8919fea34c05871592275c86bc56' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1069&endYear=1069')">1069年</a>　迁翰林学士、知开封府。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1069&endYear=1069')">1069年10月</a>　上《论制科之士不可以直言弃黜状》<div id='poem_1169112' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169112' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169112?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论制科之士不可以直言弃黜状<span class='inlineComment2'>（熙宁二年十月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1069年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34428, "北宋", "韩维", "poem_title_1169112")'>韩维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169112_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169112'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169112'>臣伏见应贤良方正举孔文仲对策入等，以论时政意异，诏文仲罢归。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169112_comment'></div>仰惟陛下导人使言，一有不合，便行弃黜，此后谁敢有言者？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169112_comment'></div>陛下尝嫉言事之人好同流俗，沮败朝廷行事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169112_comment'></div>且行事在审理，审理在合时变，使流言自息，乃为善也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169112_comment'></div>而欲黜责以止之，臣见其无益于行事，有损于治道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169112_comment'></div>陛下毋以文仲为一贱士而黜之，何损于事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169112_comment'></div>古人于事常戒微渐，臣恐贤俊由此解体，忠良结舌，阿谀茍合之人得窥其间而兢进，为祸不细。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169112_comment'></div>文仲可取而逐之，臣恐于文仲未有所损，而其损顾在陛下也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169112_comment'></div>顾改赐处分，以幸天下。</div><div id='poem_sentence_8_1169112_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1069&endYear=1069')">1069年10月</a>　上《议贡举状》<div id='poem_1169076' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169076' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169076?labeling=true' target='_blank'>议贡举状<span class='inlineComment2'>（熙宁二年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1069年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34428, "北宋", "韩维", "poem_title_1169076")'>韩维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169076_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169076'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169076'>右臣伏奉敕命，议考校贡举之法者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169076_comment'></div>臣谨按《周礼》大司徒之职，以乡三物教万民而<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_1_1169076", 1169076, "Clauses/3/Comments/0")'>宾兴</span>之，曰六德，曰六行，曰六艺，所以修身事君，事父母，接兄弟、亲戚、朋友、乡党之道，无不教也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169076_comment'></div>至于射御书数，亦皆时所资用，无非事而为之者，故起而仕之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169076_comment'></div>则其所施设者，皆素业也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169076_comment'></div>今之士固未尝教也，而又诱之以华靡无用之文，程之以诵记不讲之言，至于行能则漫然不省矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169076_comment'></div>故及其仕也，平居之所先务者，今则无所施矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169076_comment'></div>前日之所力习者，今则不足用矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169076_comment'></div>其所以时得贤俊之士而官之者，幸也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169076_comment'></div>今欲讲图善法，以变其习俗，则当先去其无益者，而使就其益者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1169076_comment'></div>臣请以五事言之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1169076_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_1169076'>一、罢诗赋，更令于所习一大经中<span class='inlineComment2'>（令人通习某经。）</span>问大义十道，但以文辞解释，不必全记注疏，取其言典雅得圣人之意者，通七以上为合格。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1169076_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_1169076'>一、本设明经，举其所取人数与诸科相通者，亦欲渐诱经生，使习义理之学。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1169076_comment'></div>而比来中选尚少，盖进士患于不能记诵，诸科患于不能解释。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1169076_comment'></div>今请少损贴墨之数，以来进士。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1169076_comment'></div>所放诸科既少，则其翘然者必须力学以趋此举。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1169076_comment'></div>又诸科试大义常在末场，多是合格人数已定，虽有大义不中程，亦难复黜落<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1169076_comment'></div>今请稍移大义在前，黜其不通者，则诵记者不得专进。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1169076_comment'></div>此皆所以儆厉诸科，使渐就明经也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1169076_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_18_1169076'>一、州府军监诸学，每生徒百人以上<span class='inlineComment2'>（生徒数以秋赋就试人为准。）</span>，特置教授官一员；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1169076_comment'></div>不及百人，以职官若曹官兼领<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑵</sup>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1169076_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_20_1169076'>一、每当解发，自知州至凡当职官吏，及虽非当职而仕者，及虽不仕而以道艺处乡里者，并应举人，大会州之听事，或学之讲堂，令众评行义尤异者，以品目高下书为一状<span class='inlineComment2'>（无尤异者听勿举。）</span>，俟程试定合格人数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1169076_comment'></div>如所举人在得中者，升其名于上列，仍以名移南省，试日稍加优异<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑶</sup>殿试亦如之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1169076_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_22_1169076'>一、于常试之外，别开数语，如近岁敦遣之比，其人材系自朝廷所欲得者，临时命科。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1169076_comment'></div>凡此皆变旧法之尤无益者，而稍加奖厉之道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1169076_comment'></div>若夫道德贵于朝廷，则下知所慕矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1169076_comment'></div>教化明于太学，则四方有所成矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1169076_comment'></div>惟在陛下与一二执政之臣力行而详处之，则明诏所谓「一道德而奖进人材」，斯无难矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1169076_comment'></div>谨具状奏闻，伏候敕旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_27_1169076_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1169076'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_15_1169076_0'>⑴ 今试大义，条中有不指义理，而但引注疏，备为通，及六分为粗，当更改。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_19_1169076_0'>⑵ 教授官为两制、三馆、国子监官杂举，籍其名，遇其阙则授之。</div></div><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_21_1169076_0'>⑶ ，优异法别当议。</div></div></div><div id='poem_note_1169076_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1069&endYear=1069')">1069年10月</a>　上《乞不受尊号劄子》<div id='poem_1169077' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169077' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169077?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞不受尊号劄子<span class='inlineComment2'>（熙宁二年）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1069年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34428, "北宋", "韩维", "poem_title_1169077")'>韩维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169077_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169077'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169077'>臣昨日伏睹中书劄子下礼院，以四月一日拜表上尊号。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169077_comment'></div>臣伏以尊号者，非起于治古，而生于后世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169077_comment'></div>人君之侈心，平居为之，已累谦光；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169077_comment'></div>施于寅畏消复之日，更于义理有害。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169077_comment'></div>何则？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169077_comment'></div>比年以来，地震几遍天下，而河北尤为特甚，自前史故老所传，罕有若此之异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169077_comment'></div>加以冬无宿雪，春无嘉雨，寒暄晦明，反理失节。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169077_comment'></div>今兹河北地震尚未止，流民尚未复，畿甸诸道尚有未得雨处，而都下风霾日夕发作，乃欲以此时褒功德，崇上徽号，臣窃以为非其时矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169077_comment'></div>且陛下忧闵旱暵，遍祷于天地庙社之祠，计其祝文，必须引咎谢谴。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1169077_comment'></div>嘉应未答，而遽举推崇之礼，虽陛下冲挹，未必当之，然而事理相反有异，诚恐不足以动天消变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1169077_comment'></div>假使此事是圣意切所欲得，犹当痛自损抑，以答天戒。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1169077_comment'></div>况陛下兼帝皇而称之，尚何顾此数字之美乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1169077_comment'></div>伏望圣慈，深思灾变之大，务以至诚为本，亟出手诏，推而勿受。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1169077_comment'></div>臣愚戆，但知有益人君则为之，不识忌讳，惟陛下宽其罪而收其意，则天下之幸，非臣之幸。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1169077_comment'></div>取进止。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1169077_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1070&endYear=1070')">1070年4月</a>　复知开封府，兼侍读学士,充群牧使。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1070&endYear=1070')">1070年7月</a>　以越王德昭世程、宗惠不应封事，韩维等再议官各罚铜三十斤。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1070&endYear=1070')">1070年9月</a>　上《乞开封府四厢依旧存留使臣管勾役事奏》<div id='poem_1169114' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169114' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169114?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞开封府四厢依旧存留使臣管勾役事奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（熙宁三年九月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1070年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34428, "北宋", "韩维", "poem_title_1169114")'>韩维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169114_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169114'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169114'>逐厢旧置勾当使臣四员，今并减罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169114_comment'></div>其开陶渠堑，委都水监。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169114_comment'></div>救应人户火烛，委巡检司。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169114_comment'></div>自馀事件，即令勾当四厢京朝官依使臣例管勾勘会。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169114_comment'></div>四厢公事，惟检覆抄劄，打量界至，检定贼纵由往，福田院支贫子钱，最是奔走不完。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169114_comment'></div>若令所置京朝官逐时躬亲点检事头，区断公事，窃虑有所妨阙。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169114_comment'></div>乞逐厢依旧存留使臣，分管前项奔走之役。</div><div id='poem_sentence_6_1169114_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1070&endYear=1070')">1070年10月</a>　上《陕西义勇分番屯戍奏》<br /><a href="javascript: class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34428, "北宋", "韩维", "poem_title_1169115")'>韩维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169115_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169115'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169115'>本府衙司投名及乡户、衙前等人数差遣不均，良民颇受其害，益由条例繁杂，猾吏缘以舞弄。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169115_comment'></div>今相度减罢本府乡户、衙前八百三十五人，总减重难十八万一千馀缗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169115_comment'></div>其诸处勾当，或召税户及诸色人，或就差见充押录，或创差三司军将，或更不差人。</div><div ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1071&endYear=1071')">1071年3月</a>　上《乞候农闲排定保甲奏》<div id='poem_1169116' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169116' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1168800_comment'></div>遽阅奏功，有殊期待。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1168800_comment'></div>尚勉修于军务，奚过恤于人言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1168800_comment'></div>汝惟竭忠，朕不忘善。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1168800_comment'></div></div><div id='poem_sentence_5_1168800_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='6bb9444c966644eda410b683fd774778_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("6bb9444c966644eda410b683fd774778");'><span id='6bb9444c966644eda410b683fd774778_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1071&endYear=1072')">1071-1072年</a>，55-56岁</div><div id='6bb9444c966644eda410b683fd774778' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1071&endYear=1071')">1071年</a>　与邵雍交游唱和。作品：《和微之尧夫作会》《和尧夫思湖上秋时见寄》《陪尧夫兄弟一饭清话》《谢尧夫寄新酒》《寓展江亭谢尧夫寄酒及花》《再和尧夫同前二首》<div id='poem_244396' class='_poem'><div class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34428, "北宋", "韩维", "poem_title_244396")'>韩维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_244396_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_244396'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_244396'>燕豆何频设，归鞍夜屡阑。<div id='poem_sentence_0_244396_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_244396'>敢言挥麈倦，惟怯釂觞难。<div id='poem_sentence_1_244396_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_244396'>就暖歌筵密，凭高绘境宽。<div id='poem_sentence_2_244396_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_244396'>未甘闲处卧，犹学少时欢。<div id='poem_sentence_3_244396_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_244396'>浮蚁凌山玉，飞花掩袖纨<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：《雪赋》云纨袖惭冶。）</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_4_244396_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_244396'>幸同诸老醉，击壤颂安安。<div id='poem_sentence_5_244396_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_244396'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_244396_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_244188' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_244188' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a id='poem_content_244188'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_244188'>落尽芙蕖十顷红，败荷衰草满秋风。<div id='poem_sentence_0_244188_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_244188'>夷犹画鹢来天外，嘹唳惊鸿入镜中。<div id='poem_sentence_1_244188_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_244188'>亭榭装成如待我，樽罍开处便思翁。<div id='poem_sentence_2_244188_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_244188'>粗官岂得君留滞，府第深严合在东。<div id='poem_sentence_3_244188_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_content_497509'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_497509'>相别相逢似转轮，迹虽辽远意常亲。<div id='poem_sentence_0_497509_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_497509'>美羹旧手钦元老，盐菜诚心待故人<sup class='reference inlineComment2'>⑴</sup>。<div id='poem_sentence_1_497509_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_497509'>密竹环波宁受暑，残花映叶尚留春。<div id='poem_sentence_2_497509_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_497509'>逍遥竟日闻嘉话，时节方知自有因。<div id='poem_sentence_3_497509_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_497509'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_497509_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_497509'><div class='inline1'><div id='poem_sentence_1_497509_0'>⑴ 自注：梁柳为阳城守，过皇甫谧，谧之门人欲厚具待之，谧曰：予平日待梁柳不过盐菜，今而厚其，是贵阳城太守而贱梁柳也。待之如初。</div></div></div><div
