href='/Writing/1169074?labeling=true' target='_blank'>议僖祖庙状<span class='inlineComment2'>（熙宁五年四月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1072年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34428, "北宋", "韩维", "poem_title_1169074")'>韩维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169074_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169074'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169074'>准敕，准中书门下奏：「准治平四年闰三月八日敕，迁僖祖庙主藏之夹室。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169074_comment'></div>臣等闻万物本于天，人本乎祖，故先王庙祀之制，有疏而无绝，有追而无遗。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169074_comment'></div>商周之王断自稷契以下者，非绝帝喾以上而遗之，以其自有本统承之故也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169074_comment'></div>若夫尊卑之位，先后之序，则子孙虽自齐圣有功，不得以私其祖考，天下万世之通道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169074_comment'></div>窃以本朝自僖祖以上世次不可得而知，则僖祖有庙，于契稷无以异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169074_comment'></div>今毁其庙而藏其主夹室，替祖考之尊，下附于子孙，殆非所以顺祖宗孝心、事亡如存之义。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169074_comment'></div>求之前代，虽或有之，然考合于经，乃无成说。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169074_comment'></div>因情制礼，实在圣时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169074_comment'></div>伏惟皇帝陛下，仁孝聪明，绍天稽古，动容周旋，惟道之从。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1169074_comment'></div>宗庙重事，所宜博考，乞以所奏付之两府详议而择取其当」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1169074_comment'></div>奉敕旨准今月三日诏：「中书门下：庙祧之制，盖闻彝典，所以上承先王，下法后世。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1169074_comment'></div>朕嗣宅大统，敬奉宗祀，而世次迁毁，礼或未安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1169074_comment'></div>讨论经常属二三哲辅，于以佐朕不逮，而仰称祖宗追孝之心。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1169074_comment'></div>今览之瞿然，敢不祇服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1169074_comment'></div>宜依所请施行。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1169074_comment'></div>故兹诏示，想宜知悉」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1169074_comment'></div>牒奉诏书如前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1169074_comment'></div>牒至，准诏书者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1169074_comment'></div>伏惟亲亲之序，以三为五，以五为九，上杀下杀，旁及而亲毕。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1169074_comment'></div>圣人制事，存送终之礼，皆以此为限，是众人之所同也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1169074_comment'></div>若其不与众人同者，则又因事之宜，断之以义，而为之节文也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1169074_comment'></div>昔先王既有天下，迹其基业之所由起，奉以为太祖，所以推功美，重本始也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1169074_comment'></div>盖王者之祖有系天下者矣，诸侯之祖有系一国者矣，大夫士之祖有系一家者矣，亦其理势然也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1169074_comment'></div>荀卿曰：「王者天，太祖，诸侯不敢坏，大夫士有常宗，所以别贵始」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1169074_comment'></div>贵始，德之本也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1169074_comment'></div>盖有天下之始若后稷，有一国之始若周公，大夫士之始若三桓。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1169074_comment'></div>所以贵者，配天也，不祧也，有常宗也，此其所以别也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1169074_comment'></div>今直以契稷为本统之祖，则是下同大夫士之礼，非荀卿之所谓别也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1169074_comment'></div>或曰：「汤、文、武之去契、稷，皆十有馀世，其间子孙衰微奔窜者非一，汤、文、武之有天下，契、稷何与哉」？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1169074_comment'></div>曰：南宫适曰：「禹、稷躬稼而有天下」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1169074_comment'></div>孔子曰：「君子哉若人」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1169074_comment'></div>禹之有天下则然矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1169074_comment'></div>稷，诸侯也，而曰「有天下」，何哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1169074_comment'></div>岂非积累功德，至文王而兴乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1169074_comment'></div>孟子曰：「王不待大，汤以七十里，文王以百里」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1169074_comment'></div>然则小国亦王之所待也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1169074_comment'></div>所谓「七十里」「百里」者，非契、稷所受以遗其子孙之国乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1169074_comment'></div>由是言之，商、周所以兴，契、稷不为无所与也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1169074_comment'></div>则正考父作《颂》追道「契汤高宗，商所以兴」，子夏序《诗》称「文武之功，起于后稷」，岂虚语也哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1169074_comment'></div>《国语》亦曰：「契勤，商十有四世而兴；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1169074_comment'></div>后稷勤，周十有五世而兴」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1169074_comment'></div>《谷梁》曰：「始封必为祖」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1169074_comment'></div>南宫适、孟轲、卜子夏、左丘明、谷梁赤生于周代，其所言者，皆亲闻而见之者，其学问又俱出于孔子，宜若可信。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1169074_comment'></div>则尊始祖以其功之所起，秦、汉诸儒亦有所受之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_43_1169074_comment'></div>后世有天下者，皆特起，无所因，故遂为一代之太祖，所从来久矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_44_1169074_comment'></div>伏惟太祖皇帝孝友仁圣，睿智神武，兵不血刃，坐清大乱，子孙<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_45_1169074", 1169074, "Clauses/156/Comments/0")'>遵业</span>，万世蒙泽，功德卓然，为宋太祖，无少议者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_45_1169074_comment'></div>僖祖虽于太祖高祖也，然仰迹功业，未见其有所因；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_46_1169074_comment'></div>上寻世系，又不知所以始。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_47_1169074_comment'></div>若以所事稷、契奉之，窃恐于古无考，而于今有所未安也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_48_1169074_comment'></div>臣以为均之论议，未有以相夺，仍旧便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_49_1169074_comment'></div>若夫藏主合食，则历代常议之矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_50_1169074_comment'></div>然今之庙室与古殊制，古者每庙异宫，今所以奉祖宗者皆在一堂之上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_51_1169074_comment'></div>西夹室犹处顺祖之右，考之尊卑之次，似亦无嫌。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_52_1169074_comment'></div>至于禘祫，自是序昭穆之祭，僖祖东向，礼无不顺，所谓子虽齐圣，不先父食者也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_53_1169074_comment'></div>孔子曰：「于其所不知，盖阙如也」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_54_1169074_comment'></div>如臣绛等议，非臣所知，臣所以阙而不敢同也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_55_1169074_comment'></div></div><div class='poemNote' id='poem_note_1169074'><span class='label'>按：</span>《南阳集》卷二五。又见《续资治通鉴长编》卷二四○，《皇朝文鉴》卷一○五，《宋会要辑稿》礼一五之三八。第一册第六七○页《国朝诸臣奏议》卷八七，《宋史》卷一○六，《历代名臣奏议》卷二○，《右编》卷三四，《文章辨体汇选》卷一五二，《经济类编》卷四○，《古今图书集成》礼仪典卷二二八。<br /></div><div id='poem_note_1169074_comment'></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1072&endYear=1072')">1072年6月</a>　拟《赐新除守太傅检校太师兼侍中河阳三城节度使致仕曾公亮辞免致仕恩命不允诏》<div id='poem_1168810' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1168810' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1168810?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐新除守太傅检校太师兼侍中河阳三城节度使致仕曾公亮辞免致仕恩命不允诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1072年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34428, "北宋", "韩维", "poem_title_1168810")'>韩维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1168810_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1168810'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1168810'>朝廷待将相之臣，其礼秩宠数，皆有成律，著在简策。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1168810_comment'></div>若夫议勋旧之美，酌报礼之称；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1168810_comment'></div>则又有加焉，此典制也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1168810_comment'></div>卿以德义经术弼亮三世，于其归也，礼秩之数，宜在加等。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1168810_comment'></div>过自损挹，非所望也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1168810_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1072&endYear=1072')">1072年6月</a>　拟《赐河阳三城节度使守司空检校太师兼侍中曾公亮乞致仕不允批答》<div id='poem_1168835' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1168835' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1168835?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐河阳三城节度使守司空检校太师兼侍中曾公亮乞致仕不允批答</a><span class='authorDate'>（1072年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34428, "北宋", "韩维", "poem_title_1168835")'>韩维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1168835_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1168835'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1168835'>古之人虽云「七十而致仕」，至于勋德耆艾，朝所倚用，盖有不得谢者矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1168835_comment'></div>卿沉雄之度，明审之略，宣力左右，厥庸茂焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1168835_comment'></div>朕方赖卿老谋，咨以赋事，而遽欲引年而去，岂朕所以待勋德之意哉？</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1168835_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1072&endYear=1072')">1072年6月</a>　拟《赐河阳三城节度使守司空检校太师兼侍中曾公亮乞致仕第二表不允批答》<div id='poem_1168836' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1168836' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1168836?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐河阳三城节度使守司空检校太师兼侍中曾公亮乞致仕第二表不允批答</a><span class='authorDate'>（1072年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34428, "北宋", "韩维", "poem_title_1168836")'>韩维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1168836_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1168836'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1168836'>朕悯以烦务，勤我耆德，故命解剧藩之政，委真廷之领。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1168836_comment'></div>燕息里第，足以造适而养安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1168836_comment'></div>虽还政之逸，不是过也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1168836_comment'></div>何嫌而欲上将相印绶，遂以去位？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1168836_comment'></div>勉即官次，用副眷怀。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1168836_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='c9ddea96b9b64c0fb7ae6ef01265f894_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("c9ddea96b9b64c0fb7ae6ef01265f894");'><span id='c9ddea96b9b64c0fb7ae6ef01265f894_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1074&endYear=1074')">1074年</a>，58岁</div><div id='c9ddea96b9b64c0fb7ae6ef01265f894' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1074&endYear=1074')">1074年2月</a>　以翰林学士承旨被召回京,知开封府。不久天降大雨,韩维作《久早喜雨》<div id='poem_244416' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_244416' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/244416?labeling=true' target='_blank'>久旱喜雨</a><span class='authorDate'>（1074年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34428, "北宋", "韩维", "poem_title_244416")'>韩维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_244416_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_244416'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_244416'>炎风驾京尘，久旱氛祲恶。<div id='poem_sentence_0_244416_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_244416'>羲和鞭日车，光焰赫飞跃。<div id='poem_sentence_1_244416_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_244416'>群生困熬暴，嘉谷坐焦灼。<div id='poem_sentence_2_244416_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_244416'>高堂袒裼卧，汗下如鞭索。<div id='poem_sentence_3_244416_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_244416'>安知于此时，乃见嘉树<span class='inlineComment2'>（疑当作澍）</span>落。<div id='poem_sentence_4_244416_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_244416'>狂飘随烟云，急洒动林薄。<div id='poem_sentence_5_244416_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_244416'>萧然宇宙间，昏雾一疏瀹。<div id='poem_sentence_6_244416_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_244416'>虽忻意暂豁，所叹施未博。<div id='poem_sentence_7_244416_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_244416'>雷霆司天令，何乃久寂寞。<div id='poem_sentence_8_244416_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_244416'>微阴虽自复，阳亢不为却。<div id='poem_sentence_9_244416_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_244416'>安得跻帝阍，一鼓造化橐。<div id='poem_sentence_10_244416_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_244416'>太上方厉政，进贤登謇谔。<div id='poem_sentence_11_244416_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_244416'>日将太平近<span class='inlineComment2'>（旧钞本作延）</span>，此变不应作。<div id='poem_sentence_12_244416_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_244416'>吾徒勿咨嗟，坐看雨时若。<div id='poem_sentence_13_244416_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_244416'></div><div id='poem_sentence_14_244416_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1074&endYear=1074')">1074年3月</a>　对延和殿。作品：《求直言诏》<div id='poem_1168796' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1168796' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1168796?labeling=true' target='_blank'>求直言诏<span class='inlineComment2'>（熙宁七年三月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1074年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34428, "北宋", "韩维", "poem_title_1168796")'>韩维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1168796_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1168796'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1168796'>朕涉道日浅，昧于致治。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1168796_comment'></div>政失厥中，以干阴阳之和，乃自冬迄春，旱暵为虐，四海之内，被灾者广。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1168796_comment'></div>间诏有司损常膳，避正殿，冀以塞责消变。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1168796_comment'></div>历日滋久，未能休应。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1168796_comment'></div>嗷嗷下民，大命近止。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1168796_comment'></div>中夜以兴，震悸靡宁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1168796_comment'></div>永惟其咎，未知攸出。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1168796_comment'></div>意者朕之听纳不得于理欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1168796_comment'></div>狱讼非其情欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1168796_comment'></div>赋歛失其节欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1168796_comment'></div>忠谋谠言郁于上闻，而阿谀壅蔽以成其私者众欤？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1168796_comment'></div>何嘉气之久不效也？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1168796_comment'></div>应中外文武臣僚，并许实封直言朝政阙失，朕将亲览，考求其当，以辅政理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1168796_comment'></div>三事大夫，其务悉心交儆，成朕志焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1168796_comment'></div>故兹诏示，想宜知悉。</div><div id='poem_sentence_14_1168796_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1074&endYear=1074')">1074年3月</a>　上《乞改命大臣祥定行人输钱免行利害》<div id='poem_1169119' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169119' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169119?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞改命大臣详定行人输钱免行利害<span class='inlineComment2'>（熙宁七年三月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1074年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34428, "北宋", "韩维", "poem_title_1169119")'>韩维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169119_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169119'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169119'>方集众行体问利害，全系纳钱多寡，须俟臣等见得的确合减分数，别降指挥。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169119_comment'></div>今如此，则是吕嘉问等所定有得而臣等所言为不足信，伏乞改命可信之人，使毕其事。</div><div id='poem_sentence_1_1169119_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1074&endYear=1074')">1074年3月</a>　上《乞镯除租税奏》作品：《乞蠲除租税奏》<div id='poem_1169120' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169120' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169120?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞蠲除租税奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（熙宁七年三月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1074年3月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34428, "北宋", "韩维", "poem_title_1169120")'>韩维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169120_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169120'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169120'>近日畿内诸县督索青苗钱甚急，往往鞭挞取足，民至伐桑为薪以易钱货。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169120_comment'></div>旱灾之际，重罹此苦。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169120_comment'></div>夫动甲兵，危士民，匮财用于荒夷之地，朝廷处之不疑，行之甚锐，至于蠲除租税，宽裕逋负，以救愁苦之良民，则迟迟而不肯发。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169120_comment'></div>望陛下自奋英断行之，过而养人，犹愈于过而杀人也。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1169120_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1074&endYear=1074')">1074年4月</a>　拟《除康公再相制》<div id='poem_1168820' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1168820' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1168820?labeling=true' target='_blank'>除康公再相制<span class='inlineComment2'>（熙宁七年四月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1074年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34428, "北宋", "韩维", "poem_title_1168820")'>韩维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1168820_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1168820'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1168820'>门下：王者临四海之广，总万机之烦，仍欲措世于治安，其在求贤而辅助。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1168820_comment'></div>我图元弼，兹得荩臣，锡以茂恩，告于列位。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1168820_comment'></div>具官韩某，受才宏博，涉道深纯，智略足以经远猷，忠嘉足以任大事。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1168820_comment'></div>而自与谋帷幄，正位钧衡。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1168820_comment'></div>抗论在前，义无曲学；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1168820_comment'></div>宣力于外，劳不辞难。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1168820_comment'></div>质于舆言，眷乃旧德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1168820_comment'></div>冠宰司之重，实赖于谟明；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1168820_comment'></div>总史观之华，更资于良直。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1168820_comment'></div>赋之多邑，衍以真封。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1168820_comment'></div>并示褒章，允为异数。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1168820_comment'></div>于呼！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1168820_comment'></div>百姓尚困，惟在厚厥生；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1168820_comment'></div>远人未宾，当使扰吾化。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1168820_comment'></div>勉辅丕丕之业，以成晏晏之风<span class='inlineComment2'>（云云）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1168820_comment'></div>主者施行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1168820_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1074&endYear=1074')">1074年4月</a>　上《恳求去位奏》。优诏答之。<div id='poem_1169121' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169121' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169121?labeling=true' target='_blank'>恳求去位奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（熙宁七年四月己卯）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1074年4月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34428, "北宋", "韩维", "poem_title_1169121")'>韩维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169121_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169121'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169121'>陛下待臣乃在吕嘉问之下，臣虽不才，先帝所命以辅陛下于初潜，行年六十，未尝有一言稍陟阿谀以须己利，未尝有一言不尽道理以塞圣聪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169121_comment'></div>今于此小事处置关防，乃不得与新进小臣为比，臣复何面目出入禁闼，称侍从官以见都城之民哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169121_comment'></div>恳求去位。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1169121_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div><div class='label1' id='612203ccb9f04814983303b80cea250f_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("612203ccb9f04814983303b80cea250f");'><span id='612203ccb9f04814983303b80cea250f_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1080&endYear=1080')">1080年</a>，64岁</div><div id='612203ccb9f04814983303b80cea250f' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1080&endYear=1080')">1080年9月</a>　为通议大夫、崇政殿学士。<br /></div><div class='label1' id='2ef2e605875b40b2ae290a240133a098_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("2ef2e605875b40b2ae290a240133a098");'><span id='2ef2e605875b40b2ae290a240133a098_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1085&endYear=1087')">1085-1087年</a>，69-71岁</div><div id='2ef2e605875b40b2ae290a240133a098' class='detail'><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1085&endYear=1085')">1085年3月</a>　神宗崩,韩维赴临闺庭,太皇太后遣中使降手诏劳问。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1085&endYear=1085')">1085年6月</a>　知陈州。未行，诏兼侍读，加大学士。作品：《上宣仁皇后论保甲保马劄子》<div id='poem_1169083' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169083' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169083?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上宣仁皇后论保甲保马劄子<span class='inlineComment2'>（元丰八年六月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1085年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34428, "北宋", "韩维", "poem_title_1169083")'>韩维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169083_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169083'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169083'>臣窃闻陛下浚发德音，斥宋用臣等出就外省，罢其所领职事；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169083_comment'></div>黜吴居厚，使离本道，责以掊刻扰民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169083_comment'></div>中外喧传，晓然知陛下忧国爱民之深意，莫不欣悦相贺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169083_comment'></div>臣虽在哀戚之中，不觉失声欢呼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169083_comment'></div>然臣尚有愚恳，不敢不尽以上闻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169083_comment'></div>臣窃恐议者以嗣君新即位，且当循守父道，三年无改。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169083_comment'></div>此大不然。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169083_comment'></div>伏惟太皇太后于大行皇帝为母仪，于今上皇帝有祖母之尊，此时称制临政，盖为社稷大计，事有不便，弛以利民，考古相时，理无不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169083_comment'></div>臣以为万一有敢为此论上惑天听者，若非奸人沮害圣政，即是俗儒不识时变，愿陛下切勿听之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1169083_comment'></div>臣近去都下日，比因进对，曾具奏陈，乞陛下深察盗贼所起之原，罢非业之令，宽训练之程，盖为保马保甲发也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1169083_comment'></div>何则？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1169083_comment'></div>农民以稼穑为生死之资，出钱市马，已非其愿；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1169083_comment'></div>又守护灌饲，素昧其方，万一死损，复更偿买。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1169083_comment'></div>昔时一马直三二十千者，今至百千矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1169083_comment'></div>农民如此，未有已时，愁叹之声，闻于道路。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1169083_comment'></div>近岁保甲筑垣为场，号为团教。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1169083_comment'></div>一丁在官训习，又须一丁供送饭食，家阙耕作，身受劳苦，不无怨怼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1169083_comment'></div>夫使失业怨怼之人操持兵器，习为击刺之事，岂不可虑？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1169083_comment'></div>近者又闻江西保马颇为群盗掠取，换易乘骑，如其外厩；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1169083_comment'></div>河北保甲渐亦作过，侵暴良民，州县不能禁。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1169083_comment'></div>此患在耳目之前，则更易措置，诚不可缓也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1169083_comment'></div>且臣非谓国马遂不可养，但国置监牧可矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1169083_comment'></div>臣非谓民兵遂不可教，但于农隙一时训练可矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1169083_comment'></div>孟子曰：「天时不如地利，地利不如人和」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1169083_comment'></div>人和可以胜天地，可不务乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1169083_comment'></div>伏望留神圣虑，详酌施行。</div><div id='poem_sentence_25_1169083_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1085&endYear=1085')">1085年6月</a>　上《进答宣问劄子》<div id='poem_1169082' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169082' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169082?labeling=true' target='_blank'>进答宣问劄子<span class='inlineComment2'>（元丰八年六月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1085年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34428, "北宋", "韩维", "poem_title_1169082")'>韩维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169082_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169082'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169082'>臣伏被圣旨曲谕诲言，退托不逮，下询愚贱，以求辅助，此诚古圣君哲后保邦安民之先务也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169082_comment'></div>臣闻命之始，且悲且喜，辄不自揆，每进瞽言，少佐初政之万一。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169082_comment'></div>窃以为治天下之道，不必过求高远，止在审人情而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169082_comment'></div>识人情不难，以己之心，推人之情，则可见矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169082_comment'></div>大凡人情，贫则思富，苦则思乐，劳则思息，郁塞则思通。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169082_comment'></div>陛下诚能以利民为本，则人富矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169082_comment'></div>以爱民为心，则人乐矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169082_comment'></div>凡事之有妨农务者去之，则劳困息矣；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169082_comment'></div>法禁之无益治道者蠲之，则郁塞通矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1169082_comment'></div>推此而广之，尽诚心而行之，则黎民赤子观陛下之法，不待教而自成，圣德贤士闻陛下之风，不烦开喻而争宣忠力矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1169082_comment'></div>何忧军民不忻戴，社稷不安固乎？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1169082_comment'></div>臣世受国恩，兄弟并列显近，陛下虽不宣谕，犹思裨补，况亲奉圣训哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1169082_comment'></div>臣无任感恩思报激切之至。</div><div id='poem_sentence_12_1169082_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1085&endYear=1085')">1085年6月</a>　上《乞删去求言诏书中六事输》<div id='poem_1169122' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169122' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169122?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞删去求言诏书中六事疏<span class='inlineComment2'>（元丰八年六月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1085年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34428, "北宋", "韩维", "poem_title_1169122")'>韩维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169122_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169122'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169122'>臣近者伏睹传录到朝堂所出榜文，开示大信，招来群言，皆前代帝王之高致，而方今朝廷之急务，天下幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169122_comment'></div>然臣尚有疑者，「若乃阴有所怀」至「不得已也」七十五字，非元谕圣旨之本意，似增饰而为之者，何则？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169122_comment'></div>前云「至于拂心逆耳犹将欣然容而不拒」，且以赏罚劝之，后所云则异于此矣，又以黜罚惧之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169122_comment'></div>且机事之重，何害密言？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169122_comment'></div>已行之令，容有未知，朝廷之意茍善，何恶其观望？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169122_comment'></div>流俗之言必浅，自可以勿听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169122_comment'></div>藉使有犯此四禁者，亦未至「拂心逆耳」，犹在「欣然容之」之列，岂可便行黜罚？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169122_comment'></div>若此言出于陛下，则是诏文前后自相违戾，疑误观者；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169122_comment'></div>若出于臣下议论，则是违异圣意，巧为辞说，以惧来者，阴成其邪志也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1169122_comment'></div>古之求言必曰「毋有所讳」，又曰「毋悼后患」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1169122_comment'></div>今则多设防禁，又以黜罚惧之，是人「有所讳」而「悼后患」也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1169122_comment'></div>古之为民者，宣之使言，下至道路刍荛亦见收采。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1169122_comment'></div>今则出榜止于朝堂，降诏不及诸道，既乖古义，亦非旧体，恐非所以推广圣德普及于遐远，开辟言路不间于幽侧也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1169122_comment'></div>此事若不改正，臣深恐自今圣德渐成壅蔽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1169122_comment'></div>臣在先帝朝，尝奉圣旨以灾旱撰《责躬求直言诏》，及下之日，都人欢悦，甘雨亦降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1169122_comment'></div>不数日，奸人希宰相意，上惑圣听，别作一诏，盖掩前诏之美，庇护新法之失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1169122_comment'></div>人情疑惧，遂不敢言，前诏但成虚文而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1169122_comment'></div>今榜后之意，颇亦类之，此事于国体不小。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1169122_comment'></div>伏望陛下深察此弊而痛绝其端，特作圣意，批降指挥，令刊去此七十五字，只以榜前所云，别撰诏文，遍颁天下，使万方之人，豁然知圣人乐善好谏之心，披云雾而睹青天白日，岂不快哉，岂不大哉！</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1169122_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1085&endYear=1085')">1085年7月</a>　兼侍读，提举中太一宫并集禧观事。作品：《乞删去求言诏书中六事输》<div id='poem_1169122' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169122' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169122?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞删去求言诏书中六事疏<span class='inlineComment2'>（元丰八年六月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1085年6月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34428, "北宋", "韩维", "poem_title_1169122")'>韩维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169122_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169122'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169122'>臣近者伏睹传录到朝堂所出榜文，开示大信，招来群言，皆前代帝王之高致，而方今朝廷之急务，天下幸甚。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169122_comment'></div>然臣尚有疑者，「若乃阴有所怀」至「不得已也」七十五字，非元谕圣旨之本意，似增饰而为之者，何则？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169122_comment'></div>前云「至于拂心逆耳犹将欣然容而不拒」，且以赏罚劝之，后所云则异于此矣，又以黜罚惧之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169122_comment'></div>且机事之重，何害密言？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169122_comment'></div>已行之令，容有未知，朝廷之意茍善，何恶其观望？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169122_comment'></div>流俗之言必浅，自可以勿听。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169122_comment'></div>藉使有犯此四禁者，亦未至「拂心逆耳」，犹在「欣然容之」之列，岂可便行黜罚？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169122_comment'></div>若此言出于陛下，则是诏文前后自相违戾，疑误观者；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169122_comment'></div>若出于臣下议论，则是违异圣意，巧为辞说，以惧来者，阴成其邪志也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1169122_comment'></div>古之求言必曰「毋有所讳」，又曰「毋悼后患」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1169122_comment'></div>今则多设防禁，又以黜罚惧之，是人「有所讳」而「悼后患」也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1169122_comment'></div>古之为民者，宣之使言，下至道路刍荛亦见收采。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1169122_comment'></div>今则出榜止于朝堂，降诏不及诸道，既乖古义，亦非旧体，恐非所以推广圣德普及于遐远，开辟言路不间于幽侧也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1169122_comment'></div>此事若不改正，臣深恐自今圣德渐成壅蔽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1169122_comment'></div>臣在先帝朝，尝奉圣旨以灾旱撰《责躬求直言诏》，及下之日，都人欢悦，甘雨亦降。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1169122_comment'></div>不数日，奸人希宰相意，上惑圣听，别作一诏，盖掩前诏之美，庇护新法之失。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1169122_comment'></div>人情疑惧，遂不敢言，前诏但成虚文而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1169122_comment'></div>今榜后之意，颇亦类之，此事于国体不小。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1169122_comment'></div>伏望陛下深察此弊而痛绝其端，特作圣意，批降指挥，令刊去此七十五字，只以榜前所云，别撰诏文，遍颁天下，使万方之人，豁然知圣人乐善好谏之心，披云雾而睹青天白日，岂不快哉，岂不大哉！</div><div id='poem_sentence_18_1169122_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1085&endYear=1085')">1085年9月</a>　上《乞依旧法禁钱币阑出边关奏》<div id='poem_1169123' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169123' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169123?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞依旧法禁钱币阑出边关奏<span class='inlineComment2'>（元丰八年九月十四日）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1085年9月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34428, "北宋", "韩维", "poem_title_1169123")'>韩维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169123_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169123'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169123'>钱币阑出边关，则足以资敌国，旧法为禁甚严。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169123_comment'></div>今每贯税钱五十文，恣听其出中国，臣请复禁如旧法。</div><div id='poem_sentence_1_1169123_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1085&endYear=1085')">1085年10月</a>　为资政殿大学士,仍依守尚书例给俸廪。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1085&endYear=1085')">1085年10月</a>　拟《赐夏国主诏》<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1085&endYear=1085')">1085年10月</a>　上《论息兵弃地劄子》<div id='poem_1169084' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169084' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169084?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论息兵弃地劄子<span class='inlineComment2'>（元丰八年十月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1085年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34428, "北宋", "韩维", "poem_title_1169084")'>韩维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169084_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169084'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169084'>臣窃见先帝时大兴甲兵，西讨夏国，始以问罪为名，既亦收其土地，遂致夏人有词，违失恭顺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169084_comment'></div>夷狄之俗，以不报仇恶为耻。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169084_comment'></div>今其国力渐复，必来攻取故地。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169084_comment'></div>若不幸复为夺去，则先帝累年劳师所得，一旦失之，已为可耻；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169084_comment'></div>若兴师拒战，则边隙自此复开，兵连祸结，未有已时。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169084_comment'></div>臣窃思兵之不可不息者三，地之不可不弃者五，请为陛下陈之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169084_comment'></div>伏惟皇帝春秋尚富，太皇太后深居九重，岂尝习闻军旅之事？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169084_comment'></div>万一寇兵犯塞，调食发兵，应接不暇，或恐震惊上心，焦劳圣虑，此兵之不可不息一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169084_comment'></div>自灵州之役，永洛之败，关陕地方彫耗，士气未复，今若再兴大役，必有失律之卒散而为盗贼者，外虞方作，内患又起，臣恐国家之忧不在夏国，此兵之不可不息二也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1169084_comment'></div>绵地千里，屯兵数十万，必藉沉谋重望之臣为之筹画，忠义拳勇之将出当战斗，干事宣力之臣千里馈粮。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1169084_comment'></div>历数见在之臣，复推近事之验，恐未易得充此任者，而又兵械皆捐弃之馀，帑庾有空乏之忧，此兵之不可不息三也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1169084_comment'></div>先帝以秉常膺朝廷爵命，而国母擅行囚废，故发兵问罪。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1169084_comment'></div>今国母已死，秉常复位，所为恭顺，有蕃臣之礼。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1169084_comment'></div>若于此时复其故地，则神宗问罪之名不为虚举，陛下赐地之意实成先志，此地之不可不弃一也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1169084_comment'></div>朝廷自得熙河之地，岁费缗钱五六百万，后拔兰州，又费百万以上。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1169084_comment'></div>所得愈多，所费愈广，招徕而无利，亦已明矣，此地之不可不弃二也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1169084_comment'></div>议者又以为兰州趋夏人巢穴至近，最为形胜，自今相度要会，可以增置城堡，弃之非便。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_16_1169084_comment'></div>陛下欲再兴师旅收复灵夏之地，则存之可也；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_17_1169084_comment'></div>若无此意，劳人费财，以奉空虚之地，则是又添一熙河也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_18_1169084_comment'></div>伏见陛下以清净为心，仁惠为政，窃恐此事不当更兴于今日，此地之不可不弃三也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_19_1169084_comment'></div>辽、夏二国世为婚姻，且有唇齿之势，万一辽国贻书援先帝兴师之意，以梁氏死、秉常复位为其请所失之地，则先得我之正理而又夺我之机会矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_20_1169084_comment'></div>此时朝廷欲弃地，则是听辽国之命而恩归于彼；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_21_1169084_comment'></div>若不与，则彰先帝之过，失大国之信，而边患复兴矣，此地之不可不弃四也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_22_1169084_comment'></div>中国之所以为可贵者，为有礼义恩信也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_23_1169084_comment'></div>夷狄之可贱者，以其贪狠暴虐也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_24_1169084_comment'></div>今操可贵以临所贱，则中国尊；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_25_1169084_comment'></div>与其所欲以成吾所不欲，则夷狄服。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_26_1169084_comment'></div>此地之不可不弃五也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_27_1169084_comment'></div>臣闻古公亶父居豳，为夷狄所攻欲得地与民。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_28_1169084_comment'></div>民皆怒，欲战。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_29_1169084_comment'></div>古公不忍，乃去豳而居于岐山之下，邠人举国扶携老弱从公于岐下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_30_1169084_comment'></div>旁国闻古公行仁，亦多归之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_31_1169084_comment'></div>古公，周之先也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_32_1169084_comment'></div>其后世因其仁爱得民，至于文、武，遂有天下。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_33_1169084_comment'></div>今乃夺人之地，又欲杀人之父兄而守之，与古人异矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_34_1169084_comment'></div>陛下试计修德行仁之效，与用兵拓地之利孰为多少？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_35_1169084_comment'></div>诚能于此时特降明诏，尽以向者所得之地赐还夏国，则其君长荷陛下之恩意，人民感朝廷之惠泽。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_36_1169084_comment'></div>至于邻敌闻中国之行仁政，吾民与兵知人主之惜民命，其欢忻之声，戴荷之心，将有甚焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_37_1169084_comment'></div>伏惟陛下鉴古公之修德，亮愚臣之忠计，发自诚心，断而行之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_38_1169084_comment'></div>臣料不独夷狄感悦，上天鉴德助顺，亦且福佑无疆矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_39_1169084_comment'></div>《书》曰：「惟德动天」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_40_1169084_comment'></div>又曰：「至诚感神，矧兹有苗」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_41_1169084_comment'></div>此皆前代圣王行之已有成效，愿陛下勿疑。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_42_1169084_comment'></div>若夫计已往之费，吝难保之地，耗金帛，动兵甲，以争不可知之胜负，而且有后患，皆世俗之常谈，岂足为陛下道哉！</div><div id='poem_sentence_43_1169084_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1085&endYear=1085')">1085年10月</a>　上《再乞息兵弃地劄子》<div id='poem_1169085' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169085' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169085?labeling=true' target='_blank'>再乞息兵弃地劄子<span class='inlineComment2'>（元丰八年十月）</span></a><span class='authorDate'>（1085年10月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34428, "北宋", "韩维", "poem_title_1169085")'>韩维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169085_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169085'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169085'>臣近具奏陈论兵之不可不息者三，地之不可不弃者五，利害甚明，极有义理。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169085_comment'></div>窃恐边防之机会或未尽经圣虑，乃不避喋喋，再有陈述。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169085_comment'></div>且思当今所宜，无出此策，愿陛下详览而深思之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169085_comment'></div>若争地用兵，则向后患祸不可知矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169085_comment'></div>陛下若发诚心以息兵爱民为意，自足以动天感人，亦不须待其来请地然后赐之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169085_comment'></div>又古人以禽兽待夷狄，但当自计利害，不当与之校也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169085_comment'></div>臣窃谓朝廷今日未是用兵劳人之时，前代圣王屈于夷狄非一，皆是此意。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169085_comment'></div>今之所处，义理甚高，非有屈也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169085_comment'></div>又臣今所言，须及时为之乃可，若夏国兴兵来犯塞，北虏贻书为请地，则失我机会，不可用矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1169085_comment'></div>古人修德行仁，不计一时利害，何则？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1169085_comment'></div>修德行仁之功大，世俗所计利害小，相去如天地之远。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1169085_comment'></div>又臣此策可以实先帝问罪之意，广陛下行仁之德，内慰士民之心，外消夷狄之患，愿陛下速行，天下幸甚。</div><div id='poem_sentence_11_1169085_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年1月</a>　上《乞不进读祖宗时事难以通变于后世者奏》<div id='poem_1169125' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169125' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169125?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞不进读祖宗时事难以通变于后世者奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（元祐元年正月丁巳）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34428, "北宋", "韩维", "poem_title_1169125")'>韩维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169125_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169125'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169125'>臣等见进读《三朝宝训》，其间有祖宗时事与今不同者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169125_comment'></div>盖当是时，天下初定，与治平之后事体自别，君臣论议亦从而异。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169125_comment'></div>又有祖宗一时处分，难以通行于后世者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169125_comment'></div>欲乞遇有似此等事，特许臣等看详，更不进读。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1169125_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年2月</a>　与吕大防等详定役法。作品：上《乞褒显范镇首倡建储之功奏》<div id='poem_1169126' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169126' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169126?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞褒显范镇首倡建储之功奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（元祐元年二月丁卯）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34428, "北宋", "韩维", "poem_title_1169126")'>韩维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169126_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169126'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169126'>臣窃见光禄大夫致仕范镇往在仁宗朝常为谏官，是时，仁宗皇帝春秋渐高，国嗣未立，中外臣庶咸以为忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169126_comment'></div>独镇率先群臣，首倡大议，择宗室之贤预建储副，以安国本。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169126_comment'></div>凡上章者十九，《贻执政书》者二，献《大合祭赋》者一，所言忠切，至忘其身。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169126_comment'></div>言未见用，则乞罢谏职，又乞放归田里，又乞降知小州。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169126_comment'></div>除知杂御史，又固辞不受，惟以安宗庙社稷为忧。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169126_comment'></div>自此大臣始继有论奏。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169126_comment'></div>英宗皇帝遂自藩邸入继大统。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169126_comment'></div>先帝追录忠信，如文彦博、富弼，皆身被褒宠，赏延其嗣，刘沆、王尧臣虽已殁，犹推恩官其子，而恩赏独不及镇。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169126_comment'></div>镇之为人忠实静默，未尝以此事语人，人亦莫为言者。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1169126_comment'></div>盖颜渊之无伐善，介子推之不言禄，镇皆有焉。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1169126_comment'></div>臣窃伤镇抱大忠，发大计，当先帝褒叙忠勋，遗不见录；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1169126_comment'></div>遭遇陛下惟新之政，耆旧退废之人毕见收采，而镇老矣，不及于用。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1169126_comment'></div>伏望圣慈，察镇先识首议，有劳宗社，特降明诏，褒显厥功。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1169126_comment'></div>使天下知朝廷之行信赏，虽久而不废；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1169126_comment'></div>人臣之抱忠计，虽隐而必录。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1169126_comment'></div>足使为善者劝，上助风化。</div><div id='poem_sentence_15_1169126_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年5月</a>　以资政殿大学士韩维为门下侍郎。为仪仗使。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年8月6日</a>　上《乞不以执政避嫌妨用人材奏》<div id='poem_1169127' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169127' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169127?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞不以执政避嫌妨用人材奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（元祐元年八月六日）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34428, "北宋", "韩维", "poem_title_1169127")'>韩维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169127_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169127'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169127'>朝廷选执政，本以进达贤能为职，今乃以执政妨用人，不可。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169127_comment'></div>方今人材难得，幸而有可用之人，又以执政故退罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169127_comment'></div>若七八执政各避私嫌，甚妨贤路，且多存形迹，非大公之道。</div><div id='poem_sentence_2_1169127_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年10月</a>　上《论内降奏》<div id='poem_1169128' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169128' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169128?labeling=true' target='_blank'>论内降奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（元祐元年十月丙戌）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34428, "北宋", "韩维", "poem_title_1169128")'>韩维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169128_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169128'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169128'>仁宗宽仁，每若近习贵戚倖求恩泽，宣谕执政：「卿等但依公执奏，可以寝罢」。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169128_comment'></div>臣备位执政，自可执奏，不敢避人怨憎。</div><div id='poem_sentence_1_1169128_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年11月</a>　上《乞诏刑部修立情法轻重等条律》<div id='poem_1169129' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169129' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169129?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞诏刑部修立情法轻重等条律</a><span class='authorDate'>（元祐元年十一月丙子）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34428, "北宋", "韩维", "poem_title_1169129")'>韩维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169129_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169129'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169129'>天下奏案必断于大理，详议于刑部，然后上之中书，决于人主。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169129_comment'></div>近岁有司或昧于知法，或便于营己，但因州郡所请，依违其言，即上中书贴黄例取旨，故四方奏谳日多于前。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169129_comment'></div>欲望刑清事省，难矣。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169129_comment'></div>今具修立到条，大理寺每受天下奏到刑名疑虑，情理可悯，情重法轻，法重情轻公案，须分明铺坐疑虑、可悯、情法重轻等条。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169129_comment'></div>若无上项情状，即具合用敕律何条断遣，刑部看详，次第申省取旨。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1169129_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1086&endYear=1086')">1086年11月</a>　上《乞每近大礼仍依常时决遣狱讼奏》<div id='poem_1169130' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169130' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169130?labeling=true' target='_blank'>乞每近大礼仍依常时决遣狱讼奏</a><span class='authorDate'>（元祐元年十一月丙子）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34428, "北宋", "韩维", "poem_title_1169130")'>韩维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169130_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169130'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169130'>请自今每近大礼，令刑部大理寺、开封府公事并依常时行遣，更不减促日限。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169130_comment'></div>罪人情欸重在害理难宽释者，别为一等，从上奏断。</div><div id='poem_sentence_1_1169130_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年2月</a>　撰皇太后册文。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年5月</a>　上《上太皇太后论罢张舜民御使职事》<div id='poem_1169131' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1169131' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1169131?labeling=true' target='_blank'>上太皇太后论罢张舜民御史职事</a><span class='authorDate'>（元祐二年五月己未）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34428, "北宋", "韩维", "poem_title_1169131")'>韩维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1169131_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1169131'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1169131'>臣近见台谏官于都堂，听其所言，大抵以台谏官许风闻言事，不当以一言之失便行退罢。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1169131_comment'></div>臣谕以台谏官，虽风闻言事，岂不得朝廷考察其言以知其能否而进退之？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1169131_comment'></div>文太师年过八十三，先朝旧相，名重四夷。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1169131_comment'></div>二圣曲加恩赐，不听其去。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1169131_comment'></div>而新进御史以所无之事形于奏诋，致其有言。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1169131_comment'></div>太皇太后若不为主张，使其忿恨引去，岂不于恩礼前后不相称？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1169131_comment'></div>而又失一威望大臣，可不惜哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1169131_comment'></div>御史以失言之故罢其职事，尚带馆职，釐务京师，其为责岂不甚薄！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_7_1169131_comment'></div>太皇太后辨大臣无实之谤，推诚加礼，以尽其心，则为大臣者宜如何报？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_8_1169131_comment'></div>其于礼岂不甚重哉！<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_9_1169131_comment'></div>又续降御批论舜民言夏国事，若听其言，岂不为国生事？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_10_1169131_comment'></div>此又义理明白，灿如日星。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_11_1169131_comment'></div>如闻台谏章疏至今未止，臣预闻国论，不能厌息浮议，致上烦圣听，日夜惶恐，甚不自安。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_12_1169131_comment'></div>然熟思之，治天下之要，惟在审义理而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_13_1169131_comment'></div>义理若明，馀非所恤。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_14_1169131_comment'></div>臣愿陛下毋以多言过劳思虑，惟在镇之而已。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_15_1169131_comment'></div>自馀诚恳，候十六日垂帘，更具面陈。</div><div id='poem_sentence_16_1169131_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1087&endYear=1087')">1087年7月</a>　罢门下侍郎。为资政殿大学士、知邓州。刘颁作《寄韩持国》，维依韵和之。作品：《依韵和贡父见寄》<div id='poem_244391' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_244391' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/244391?labeling=true' target='_blank'>依韵和贡父见寄</a><span class='authorDate'>（1087年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34428, "北宋", "韩维", "poem_title_244391")'>韩维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'>五言排律</div></div><div id='poem_title_244391_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_244391'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_244391'>早接英豪论，常多伯仲贤。<div id='poem_sentence_0_244391_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_244391'>风尘一会合，岁月几徂迁。<div id='poem_sentence_1_244391_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_244391'>禀性成樗散，干时类凿圆。<div id='poem_sentence_2_244391_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_244391'>论心谁合者，握手子欢然。<div id='poem_sentence_3_244391_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_244391'>经训开前古，谈辞屈老先。<div id='poem_sentence_4_244391_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_244391'>春游同烂漫，醉乐屡回旋。<div id='poem_sentence_5_244391_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_244391'>乐事嗟难久，离襟怅独偏。<div id='poem_sentence_6_244391_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_244391'>驱车清汝曲，佐幕紫嵩前。<div id='poem_sentence_7_244391_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_244391'>官兴惟高咏，人生得晏眠。<div id='poem_sentence_8_244391_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_244391'>丹铅涂旧史，杖屦接幽禅。<div id='poem_sentence_9_244391_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_244391'>叹息春期失<span class='inlineComment2'>（自注：尝有此约。）</span>，淹留夕梦牵。<div id='poem_sentence_10_244391_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_244391'>非因传丽唱，何以慰劳悁。<div id='poem_sentence_11_244391_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_244391'></div><div id='poem_sentence_12_244391_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end

洛阳

-----title
襄城
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='ba2f42511465496aa69aa05118d95eb7_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("ba2f42511465496aa69aa05118d95eb7");'><span id='ba2f42511465496aa69aa05118d95eb7_link' class='switch'>—</span></a><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1046&endYear=1046')">1046年</a>，30岁</div><div id='ba2f42511465496aa69aa05118d95eb7' class='detail'><span style='margin: 0 0.5em; color: gray;'>▪</span>是年秋,韩维到襄城拜访孙永,二人一同游玩,韩维作诗记之。作品：《同曼叔游菩提寺》《同曼叔游高阳山》《和曼叔灵树相别》《发襄城寄曼叔》《颖桥路中别曼叔》《和曼叔赋断蓬见别》<div id='poem_244467' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_244467' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/244467?labeling=true' target='_blank'>同曼叔游菩提寺</a><span class='authorDate'>（1046年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34428, "北宋", "韩维", "poem_title_244467")'>韩维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_244467_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_244467'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_244467'>高城如破崖，寺带乔木古。<div id='poem_sentence_0_244467_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_244467'>禅房掩清昼，佛画剥寒雨。<div id='poem_sentence_1_244467_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_244467'>荒池野蔓合，浊水佳莲吐。<div id='poem_sentence_2_244467_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_244467'>萧条联骑游，淡薄对僧语。<div id='poem_sentence_3_244467_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_244467'>秋风日夕好，胜事从此数。<div id='poem_sentence_4_244467_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_244467'></div><div id='poem_sentence_5_244467_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_244466' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_244466' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/244466?labeling=true' id='poem_sentence_1_244466_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_244466'>烟云函两山，台殿开半壁。<div id='poem_sentence_2_244466_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_244466'>解鞍高林下，仰视怯登陟。<div id='poem_sentence_3_244466_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_244466'>苍松盘老枝，矫矫入檐隙。<div id='poem_sentence_4_244466_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_244466'>微风韵其上，落耳寒恻恻。<div id='poem_sentence_5_244466_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_244466'>枇杷两高树，中国所未识。<div id='poem_sentence_6_244466_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_7_244466'>叶间青实骈，大与蜀土敌。<div id='poem_sentence_7_244466_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_8_244466'>我来暮暮后，花草已狼籍。<div id='poem_sentence_8_244466_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_9_244466'>不见踯躅红，西岩向人碧。<div id='poem_sentence_9_244466_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_10_244466'>出门步<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_10_244466", 244466, "Clauses/20/Comments/0")'>榛荟</span>，微径不可索。<div id='poem_sentence_10_244466_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_11_244466'>援篱下幽涧，剥藓题苍石。<div id='poem_sentence_11_244466_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_12_244466'>鸟啼无定音，虎斗有遗迹。<div id='poem_sentence_12_244466_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_13_244466'>石台平挺挺，野竹瘦历历。<div id='poem_sentence_13_244466_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_14_244466'>主人尉下邑，奔走困符檄。<div id='poem_sentence_14_244466_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_15_244466'>喜我萧散人，幽奇共<span class='link' onclick='ShowWordComment("poem_sentence_15_244466", 244466, "Clauses/31/Comments/0")'>搜剔</span>。<div id='poem_sentence_15_244466_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_244438_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_244438'>薄暮跃马去，飘忽如云烟。<div id='poem_sentence_2_244438_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_244438'>毋言欢戚殊，世事举皆然。<div id='poem_sentence_3_244438_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_244438'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_244438_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_244759' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_244759' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/244759?labeling=true' target='_blank'>颍桥路中别曼叔</a><span class='authorDate'>（1046年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34428, "北宋", "韩维", "poem_title_244759")'>韩维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_244759_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_244759'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_244759'>磷磷清颍流，中截两崖断。<div id='poem_sentence_0_244759_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_244759'>架桥在城底，斗出旷平漫。<div id='poem_sentence_1_244759_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_244759'>阴风无边来，左右篷惊转。<div id='poem_sentence_2_244759_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_244759'>我行感时节，跋马重为恋。<div id='poem_sentence_3_244759_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_244759'>虽非远别戚，所恨良会散。<div id='poem_sentence_4_244759_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_5_244759'>却想置酒地，松阴野色晚。<div id='poem_sentence_5_244759_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_6_244759'></div><div id='poem_sentence_6_244759_comment'></div></div></div><div id='poem_244596' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_244596' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/244596?labeling=true' target='_blank'>和曼叔赋断蓬见别</a><span class='authorDate'>（1046年）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34428, "北宋", "韩维", "poem_title_244596")'>韩维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_244596_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_244596'><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_244596'>霜蓬飞无根，岁暮随惊风。<div id='poem_sentence_0_244596_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_1_244596'>翻翻走寒野，日以去故丛。<div id='poem_sentence_1_244596_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_2_244596'>譬如远游子，飘泊从西东。<div id='poem_sentence_2_244596_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_244596'>一感颍上别，慨叹发予衷。<div id='poem_sentence_3_244596_comment'></div></div><div class='poemSentence' id='poem_sentence_4_244596'></div><div id='poem_sentence_4_244596_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>

-----title
襄阳
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='8f9001f8611e4ab3b5198efd254c77d0_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("8f9001f8611e4ab3b5198efd254c77d0");'><span id='8f9001f8611e4ab3b5198efd254c77d0_link' href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1072&endYear=1072')">1072年7月</a>　乞为端明殿学士兼翰林侍读学士、知襄州。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1073&endYear=1073')">1073年2月</a>　拟《赐淮南节度使守司徒检校太师兼侍中判大名府韩琦不允断来章诏》<div id='poem_1168806' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1168806' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1168806?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐淮南节度使守司徒检校太师兼侍中判大名府韩琦不允断来章诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1073年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1168806'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1168806'>盖功崇者宜报之厚，劳久者当处以逸，古今之常道也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1168806_comment'></div>卿弼亮著于三世，经营达于四方。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1168806_comment'></div>相圭将钺，皆所以报也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1168806_comment'></div>至于官职之劳，不能不以累卿者，诚有所赖之也。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1168806_comment'></div>勉体勤谕，为朕少安。</div><div id='poem_sentence_4_1168806_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1073&endYear=1073')">1073年2月</a>　拟《赐淮南节度使守司徒检校太师兼侍中判大名府韩琦不允辞谢诏》<div id='poem_1168808' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1168808' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1168808?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐淮南节度使守司徒检校太师兼侍中判大名府韩琦不允辞谢诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1073年2月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34428, "北宋", "韩维", class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1168808'>卿辞将相之尊，舍别都之重，而下求列藩之适，朕岂有所爱哉？<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1168808_comment'></div>顾全属士民，被服惠政，晏然者累年矣，徒得卿重卧而镇之。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1168808_comment'></div>卿其阔略细故，爱养气体，以副朕倚属之意焉<span class='inlineComment2'>（《南阳集》卷一五。）</span>。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1168808_comment'></div></div><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_3_1168808'>焉：原无，据明钞本补。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1168808_comment'></div></div></div><br /></div>
-----end



-----title
孟州
-----detail
<div class='label1' id='b019dde149f74336b8494703a0bac308_label'><a href='javascript: DetailSwitch("b019dde149f74336b8494703a0bac308");'><span id='b019dde149f74336b8494703a0bac308_link' ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1074&endYear=1074')">1074年11月</a>　落端明殿学士。<br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1075&endYear=1075')">1075年7月</a>　拟《赐皇伯崇信军节度使知大宗正事宗旦不允辞谢诏》<div id='poem_1168812' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1168812' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1168812?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐皇伯崇信军节度使知大宗正事宗旦不允辞谢诏</a><span class='authorDate'>（1075年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34428, "北宋", "韩维", "poem_title_1168812")'>韩维</a></span><br /><div class='titleIndent'></div></div><div id='poem_title_1168812_comment'></div><div class='poemContent' id='poem_content_1168812'><div class='articleSentence' id='poem_sentence_0_1168812'>向咨耆德，内表宗藩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1168812_comment'></div>方期信厚之风，共壮磐维之势。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1168812_comment'></div>遽形奏牍，曲谕冲辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1168812_comment'></div>顾惇叙之有惭，岂恪居之为旷，勉安厥位，庸副所怀。</div><div id='poem_sentence_3_1168812_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1075&endYear=1075')">1075年7月</a>　拟《赐皇伯新除崇信军节度使宗旦辞免恩命不允批答》<div id='poem_1168831' class='_poem'><div id='poem_title_1168831' class='poemTitle showDetail'><a href='/Writing/1168831?labeling=true' target='_blank'>赐皇伯新除崇信军节度使宗旦辞免恩命不允批答</a><span class='authorDate'>（1075年7月）</span><span class='poemAuthor'><span class='inlineComment1'> 北宋 · </span><a href='javascript: ShowPoemAuthorProfile(34428, "北宋", "韩维", "poem_title_1168831")'>韩维</a></span><br /><div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_0_1168831_comment'></div>朕惟爵赏之行，本以旌德。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_1_1168831_comment'></div>苟当其任，虽亲匪私。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_2_1168831_comment'></div>秉哲含和，久而益劭；<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_3_1168831_comment'></div>信厚之教，治于宗藩。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_4_1168831_comment'></div>推叙厥劳，锡尔旌钺。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_5_1168831_comment'></div>当体公义，毋至重辞。<div class='inline' id='poem_sentence_6_1168831_comment'></div>所辞宜不允。</div><div id='poem_sentence_7_1168831_comment'></div></div></div><br /><a href="javascript: ViewDetail('scope=&author=&beginYear=1075&endYear=1075')">1075年10月</a>　复为端明殿学士、龙图阁直学士。<br /></div>
-----end
